At that time (537 B.C.), the Persian Empire stretched all the way to Asia Minor. So there was more of the Old Testament around the Mediterranean before Socrates was out of diapers than the scholars would have you believe. When Darius' decree went out, everyone in Iraq, Iran, Afghanistan, Pakistan, Syria, Armenia, Georgia, Turkey, Palestine, Lebanon, Arabia, and Egypt knew about what had taken place with Daniel. You don't think the news hopped the Hellespont into Greece, or got carried all the way to Spain by the Phoenicians?

If you want to see how "public" the events of Daniel were, look at the end of verse 26: ["his kingdom that which shall not be destroyed, and his dominion shall be even unto the end."]{.class_1922} Why, that was the conclusion of the vision of Nebuchadnezzar clear back in 2:44; it was part of Nebuchadnezzar's "testimony" back in 4:3, 34. Those Medes and Persians had heard all about what happened in Daniel 2, 3, and 4. I guarantee you that the next world empire in Nebuchadnezzar's image (Greece) was already keeping "tabs" on what the God of the Hebrews was doing there in Persia.

We have already commented on God performing signs and wonders among the Gentiles under our remarks on 4:2--3 (which see).

Verse 28 ends the historic material here in the book of Daniel. The implication from 1:21 is that Daniel served all the way into ["the first year"]{.class_1922} of Cyrus' reign. By this time, he is up in his late eighties or early nineties somewhere. We know from 10:1 that Daniel was alive and recording his prophecies all the way into Cyrus' ["third year."]{.class_1922}

Origen added the Apocryphal book of "Bel and the Dragon" to Daniel to give you Paul Harvey's "the rest of the story." Whatever numbskull wrote "Bel and the Dragon" had Daniel in the lions' den for seven days being fed by Habakkuk the prophet. The book is kind of a []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw828.xhtml_page_144}cross between Sherlock Holmes and St. George. You'll get as much out of reading Dick Tracy and Hagar the Horrible in the funnies.

No Jew living in the Promised Land ever accepted the book as Holy Scripture. Where it was accepted was by Jews living in the land where God said His name would not ["be named in the mouth"]{.class_1922} of any Jew living there: Alexandria, Egypt. It was stuck into Daniel by Theodotion (A.D. 200), and from there put into Origen's fifth column of his [Hexapla.]{.class_1921} The fifth column [is]{.class_1921} the Septuagint.

This unscriptural, non-biblical, fairy-tale nonsense was proclaimed, along with "Song of the Three Children" and "Susanna," to be part of inspired Old Testament Scripture by the Roman Catholics at the Council of Carthage in A.D. 397. All the Apocryphal books were officially sanctioned for all members of the Roman Catholic Church, under pain of [damnation]{.class_1921} ("[anathema]{.class_1921}"), at the Council of Trent (1546--1563).

Martin Luther and the [King James]{.class_1921} translators had more sense. They took them out and stuck them between the Testaments as the [writings of men]{.class_1921} that [were not inspired Scripture.]{.class_1921} Whenever you hear some apostate Fundamentalist trying to talk you out of your faith in the Book by telling you the original [King James Version]{.class_1921} had the [Apocrypha]{.class_1921} in it, he is careful not to tell you [that.]{.class_1921} Whatever Catholic "hangovers" the Reformers may have had, at least they knew what [was]{.class_1921} Holy Scripture and what [was not.]{.class_1921}

From a [devotional]{.class_1921} point of view, we can learn the following lessons from Daniel 6:

1\. The root of all sin in time and eternity is [envy]{.class_1921} (Isa. 14:12--15; Gen. 4:3--8).

2\. The Devil's main realm is [religion,]{.class_1921} not sensuality.

3\. You can be [uncompromising]{.class_1921} without being [foolish.]{.class_1921}

4\. You may go into the lions' den, but God will go with you. ["The Lion of the tribe of Juda"]{.class_1922} (Rev. 5:5) is well able to handle the ["roaring lion"]{.class_1922} trying to devour you (1 Pet. 5:8).

# Chapter 7 {.heading_67-0}

7:1 In the first year of Belshazzar king of Babylon Daniel had a dream and visions of his head upon his bed: then he wrote the dream, and told the sum of the matters.

2 Daniel spake and said, I saw in my vision by night, and, behold, the four winds of the heaven strove upon the great sea.

3 And four great beasts came up from the sea, diverse one from another.

4 The first was like a lion, and had eagle's wings: I beheld till the wings thereof were plucked, and it was lifted up from the earth, and made stand upon the feet as a man, and a man's heart was given to it.

5 And behold another beast, a second, like to a bear, and it raised up itself on one side, and it had three ribs in the mouth of it between the teeth of it: and they said thus unto it, Arise, devour much flesh.

6 After this I beheld, and lo another, like a leopard, which had upon the back of it four wings of a fowl; the beast had also four heads; and dominion was given to it.

7 After this I saw in the night visions, and behold a fourth beast, dreadful and terrible, and strong exceedingly; and it had great iron teeth: it devoured and brake in pieces, and stamped the residue with the feet of it: and it was diverse from all the beasts that were before it; and it had ten horns.

8 I considered the horns, and, behold, there came up among them another little horn, before whom there were three of the first horns plucked up by the roots: and, behold, in this horn were eyes like the eyes of man, and a mouth speaking great things.

While chapters 1--6 covered the historic material of Daniel's life and his interactions with the Kings of Babylon and Persia, chapters 7--12 cover the prophetic material given to Daniel from the reign of []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw951.xhtml_page_146}Belshazzar (chaps. 7--8) and the reigns of Darius and Cyrus (chaps. 9--12). According to the historical records, Belshazzar reigned eleven years (550--539 B.C.). Chapter 7 takes place in ["the first year"]{.class_1922} of that reign, and chapter 8 takes place in ["the third year."]{.class_1922}

But verse 1 is much more than the historic setting of the chapter. It is the key to understanding Daniel's vision in verses 3--7. All the prophetic expositors destroy the passage by making the beasts match the metals of Nebuchadnezzar's image. The assumption is that the lion matches Babylon, the bear Persia, the leopard Greece, and the last beast Rome, out of which the Antichrist arises. Even Clarence Larkin falls into the trap. But look at verse 17.

["These great beasts, which are four, are four kings, which SHALL ARISE ]{.class_1922}\[[future]{.class_1921}\][ out of the earth."]{.class_1922}

Well, if Babylon is the ["head of gold"]{.class_1922} (2:38), then the first beast (the lion) [can't]{.class_1921} be Babylon. Why not? Well, if all four beasts are future, then they arise [after]{.class_1921} the King who rules in verse 1. Belshazzar is the [last]{.class_1921} King of Babylon (5:30--31). So the first beast arises [after Babylon is gone.]{.class_1921}

That being the case, if you are going to match the beasts to the metals of the image, you have to start [after]{.class_1938} the ["head of gold."]{.class_1937-0} The [lion,]{.class_1938} therefore, wouldn't be Babylon; it would be [Persia.]{.class_1938} The [bear]{.class_1938} would be [Greece.]{.class_1938} The [leopard]{.class_1938} would be Rome. The [last beast ]{.class_1938}would be the [Antichrist's kingdom,]{.class_1938} the feet and toes of iron and clay in Nebuchadnezzar's image.

Now I have included a chart on the beasts of Daniel's vision, and there is more to them than just a repeat of the silver, brass, iron, and iron-clay of Nebuchadnezzar's image. Note, first of all, that the ["vision"]{.class_1922} is ["by night"]{.class_1922} (vs. 2). The ["night"]{.class_1922} is a picture of the Church Age (Matt. 24:43; 1 Thess. 5:1--9; Rom. 13:11--13).

Moreover, these beasts arise out of a part of the earth connected with ["the great sea"]{.class_1922} (vs. 17 cf. vss. 2--3). That ["sea"]{.class_1922} isn't the "multitude of people" of Revelation 17:15 or Isaiah 17:12--13. It's ["sea,"]{.class_1922} singular; not ["seas,"]{.class_1922} plural (Isa. 17:12). It's ["the sea,"]{.class_1922} not ["many waters"]{.class_1922} (Rev. 17:1, 15); i.e., one [specific]{.class_1921} sea---["the great sea."]{.class_1922} Throughout the Old Testament, ["the great sea"]{.class_1922} is a reference to the [Mediterranean Sea]{.class_1921} (Num. 34:6--7; Josh. 1:4, 9:1, 15:12, 47, 23:4; Ezek. 47:10, 15, 19--20, 48:28).

What you have here in this passage is a [double application.]{.class_1921} The immediate application would be to the world empires that follow Babylon. But there is a further prophetic application to kingdoms that immediately precede the Antichrist's kingdom. These kingdoms arise out of the Mediterranean. The two nations of Nebuchadnezzar's image that are surrounded by the Mediterranean on three sides are Greece and Rome. So we need to look for nations connected with those two empires that are symbolized by a lion, a bear, and a leopard. Even Larkin hints at this when he talks about the "beastly character" of "the nations" as symbolized "by their national emblems": "the [British]{.class_1921} Lion, the [Russian]{.class_1921} Bear, the [American ]{.class_1921}Eagle."

Britain was part of the Roman Empire. It has long been symbolized by a [lion;]{.class_1921} specifically, a lion [with eagle's wings]{.class_1921}---a griffin. So [Persia]{.class_1921} is a type of [England.]{.class_1921} This is significant because the two nations to send the Jews back to the Promised Land were [Persia]{.class_1921} and [England]{.class_1921} (see our comments on Ezra 1:1 in the [Bible Believer's Commentary on Ezra, Nehemiah, Esther]{.class_1921}).

The bear is a well-known symbol of [Russia,]{.class_1921} which adopted the [Greek]{.class_1921} alphabet and the [Greek]{.class_1921} Orthodox religion. So after the British Empire collapsed due to Winston Churchill giving half the land of Palestine to the Moslems (see chap. 10 of [Israel: A Deadly Piece of Dirt]{.class_1921}), Russia dominated world politics from 1950--1990. [Greece]{.class_1921} is a type of [Russia.]{.class_1921}

The leopard is an integrated beast: it has a [yellow ]{.class_1921}body (Shem), with [black]{.class_1921} spots (Ham), and a [white]{.class_1921} belly (Japheth). The Roman Empire stretched from Spain in the west and Britain in the north (Japheth), to Babylon in the east (Shem) and north Africa in the south (Ham). The nation known for integration today is [America;]{.class_1921} so [Rome]{.class_1921} is a type of [America.]{.class_1921} It is the last great world power before the []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw980.xhtml_page_149}kingdom of the Antichrist shows up. You have been watching the stage set in the last 25-plus years.

The fourth beast in verse 7 is "non-descript," but it is described in detail in Revelation 13:1--2. It is a [combination]{.class_1921} of all the other beasts; the lion, bear, and leopard are all joined into one big "multicultural" United Nations.

["And the beast which I saw was like unto a LEOPARD, and his feet were as the feet of a BEAR, and his mouth as the mouth of a LION: and the dragon gave him his power, and his seat, and great authority"]{.class_1922} (Rev. 13:2).

That's a creature made up of several animals. Do you know what the word for that in Hebrew is? It's ["behemoth"]{.class_1922} (Job 40:15)---[a plural beast.]{.class_1921} Behemoth is connected with the ["brass"]{.class_1922} and ["iron"]{.class_1922} of Nebuchadnezzar's image (Job 40:18), just as you read in Daniel 7:19.

That last beast is integrated like America, but it moves politically like Russia---Communism. Missionaries who have worked in Russia and other "Eastern Block" countries will tell you that just because the Soviet Union broke up and the Warsaw Pact dissolved, didn't mean Communism died out in those countries. A lot of those bureaucrats who served under Communism continued right on into the "new" Russia. Now (2015), Vladimir Putin, the President of Russia and a [former KGB officer,]{.class_1921} is trying to re-form the Soviet Union.

Communism is alive and well, and if you don't believe it, just go to any College campus in America. There are more Communists there teaching as professors than you will find in Russia. The government of the Antichrist will be a Communistic form of the United States. That's where Obama has been taking you for the last eight years, and there's no sign of a let-up with whoever the next President will be.

Finally, the fourth beast speaks with ["the mouth of a lion"]{.class_1922}---English. The language of commerce and travel in these last days is [English;]{.class_1921} not Spanish, Chinese, Russian, or Arabic. So God's final authority in these last days before the return of His Son is an [English]{.class_1921} Bible---the [Authorized King James Version.]{.class_1921} I didn't say there weren't good, reliable versions in other languages (like [Valera]{.class_1921} in Spanish, [Luther]{.class_1921} in German, and [Diodati]{.class_1921} in Italian). I didn't say missionaries []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw980.xhtml_page_150}should destroy the faith of their converts by correcting their Bibles with the [King James]{.class_1921} (you can teach the truth without wrecking the faith of people in the Book God gave them). I didn't say Bible-believing missionaries shouldn't give the Scriptures to their people in the native language. Don't go and say Ruckman is trying to force everyone to learn English and the [King James]{.class_1921} Bible. What I said is that Book is the [final authority]{.class_1921} in the [universal language]{.class_1921} of the last days.

You say, "But what about all the people who don't speak or read English?" What does that have to do with [final authority?]{.class_1921} From 1500 B.C. to A.D. 34, the final authority was in a language less than 1% of the world understood---Hebrew, the few passages in Aramaic notwithstanding. All these apostate hypocrites who worry about the people who don't know English---if the final authority is Hebrew and Greek, what about all the people who can't speak, read, or write those languages?

You see, the problem is not with all the people who can't read or understand English. It's not the "originals." It's apostate scholarship seeking the seat of[ final authority.]{.class_1921} They will talk you out of your faith in the Book and replace it with their opinions; from the "originals," of course, of course. So your final authority is [no book you can read or hold in your hand.]{.class_1921} They reserve to themselves the right to change [any Bible]{.class_1921} at [any time]{.class_1921} for [any reason;]{.class_1921} that goes even for the "originals" (see Sam Gipp's work on the [Variations Between Nestle's 25th, 26th, and 27th Editions]{.class_1921}).

Now there's all types of symbolism connected with these creatures. Some of them I understand (or can make an educated guess), and some I don't. I will give you what I can, and where I don't know, I'll tell you so.

That lion with the eagle's wings is England in its power. The old saying was: "The sun never sets on the British Empire." It sure did once Churchill signed those "White Papers" giving all the land of Reuben, Gad, and Manasseh (the land of "Transjordan") to Mohammed. God had the eagle's feathers plucked, and England became a third-rate nation. I am not sure about the standing on its feet ["as a man, and a man's heart given to it"]{.class_1922} (vs. 4), but it is obvious that it lost its power as a beast.

The Russian bear became the "Soviet Union" in 1922 when it took the ["three ribs"]{.class_1922} of Transcaucasia, Ukraine, and Byelorussia. There is no antecedent for the ["they"]{.class_1922} of verse 5. Larkin identifies them as the ["watchers"]{.class_1922} of 4:17. Historically, the ones who gave tacit permission to Stalin to ["devour much flesh"]{.class_1922} after World War II were "Winnie the Pooh" Churchill and FDR. So the Soviet Union took Estonia, Latvia, and Lithuania. Then it took Eastern Europe. From there, Communism spread to China, North Korea, Southeast Asia, eastern and southern Africa, and several Latin American countries.

The leopard of verse 6 has four heads and four wings. Being a type of the United States, what you have is four times the original make-up of America. This country started out with [thirteen]{.class_1921} States, so four times thirteen is [52.]{.class_1921} I have taught for years that you can expect America to end up with [52 States.]{.class_1921} I saw Alaska and Hawaii added in my lifetime; I probably won't live to see the last two. There has always been a push to make Puerto Rico and Washington, D.C. States, but I have also heard of plans to divide California into three States, which would also give you 52, a "full deck."

Notice that the wings of the leopard are not an eagle's wings, but the ["wings of a fowl"]{.class_1922}---a [chicken.]{.class_1921} I have long said that the symbol of the United States, since World War II, shouldn't be a bald eagle, but a [plucked chicken]{.class_1921} (or a nude woman).

When the Soviet Union dissolved in 1991 and America became the sole "superpower" in the world, we didn't have enough courage as a nation to liberate a country not as big as New Jersey without the help of eight other countries (Kuwait and the First Gulf War). Back in 1867, during a civil war in Cuba, an American was condemned wrongfully to die as a spy. When he went before the firing squad, the American Consul stepped in front of him, wrapped in the American flag. He said, "Shoot if you dare!" No one shot because the Cubans were afraid of what the United States government would do to their country for killing an innocent American.[ They'd shoot today.]{.class_1921} They would shoot and then burn the flag.

Under the Clintons, the Bushes, and Obama, this country has become a laughingstock. A petty Syrian dictator wasn't scared at all at Obama's "red line" against using chemical weapons against his own citizens. Iran isn't terrified at any of America's threats; it goes []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw980.xhtml_page_152}on with its plans to build a nuclear weapon to use against Israel. ISIS isn't worried one bit about anything the United States says; they just keep on taking more territory and killing more Christians. We have the wings of a [chicken,]{.class_1921} not an eagle.

Now as I told you, the last beast is an amalgamation of the three beasts preceding it; it is the same beast as the one in Revelation 13:2. That means that although only one head is mentioned here in Daniel 7 (see vs. 20), it actually has ["seven heads"]{.class_1922} (Rev. 13:1). Then it is like the Devil (Rev. 13:2), but it is different, because the Devil is ["a great dragon."]{.class_1922} Nevertheless, ["the dragon"]{.class_1922} gives this beast ["his power, and his seat, and great authority"]{.class_1922} (Rev. 13 :2). So this beast has the head of the lion (1), the head of the bear (2), the four heads of the leopard (3--6), with the seventh head being the head of the dragon (Rev. 13:2).

The last beast has ["ten horns,"]{.class_1922} matching the ten toes of Nebuchadnezzar's image in Daniel 2. So this beast is the final Gentile kingdom on this earth before Jesus Christ comes to set up His kingdom. That is exactly what follows in verse 9. But note, the beast is not just a kingdom (vs. 24); it is the King of that kingdom (vs. 17). So this last beast is the Antichrist himself.

This creature has ["great iron teeth,"]{.class_1922} connecting it with Rome, and ["nails of brass,"]{.class_1922} connecting it with Greece. Of course, if you make those the modern counterparts, they would be the United States and Russia. That is probably the case, because this creature is stomping all over everything with the bear's feet (Rev. 13:2)---Russia. That means he's devouring everything with the American teeth in the English mouth.

Now I am not sure how to put all of that together, but I can tell you at what you are looking in those iron teeth and brass nails. You have living inorganic material matching the iron-clay toes of Nebuchadnezzar's image (see our remarks on 2:43).

Now to comment on verses 7--8 adequately, we will need to go down to the interpretation given in verses 23--24, but there are certain comments on the latter passage we will reserve for when we get to it. In the meantime, look at verse 7: ["it devoured and brake in pieces, and stamped the residue with the feet of it." "Residue]{.class_1922}"of what? The verse doesn't say. You don't find out what is ["devoured"]{.class_1922} and ["stamped"]{.class_1922} until you get down to verse 23: []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw980.xhtml_page_153}["The fourth beast . . . shall devour the whole earth, and shall tread it down, and break it in pieces."]{.class_1922} The Antichrist subjugates every Gentile nation on earth. Revelation 13:7 says, ["power was given him over all kindreds, and tongues, and nations."]{.class_1922}

["It had ten horns."]{.class_1922} Verse 24 defines ["the ten horns"]{.class_1922} as ["ten kings that shall arise."]{.class_1922} Now when we get into these heads and horns, what we run into is the Devil in Revelation 12:3 as ["a great red dragon, having seven heads and ten horns, and seven crowns upon his heads."]{.class_1922} There, the Kings are the seven heads of the dragon, and there are only seven of them. That is Satan in his present state since Genesis 3. In the Bible, those Kings would be:

1\. Nimrod, the King of Babel.

2\. Pharaoh, the King of Egypt.

3\. Sennacherib, the King of Assyria.

4\. Nebuchadnezzar, the King of Babylon.

5\. Cyrus, the King of Persia.

6\. Alexander, the King of Greece.

7\. Caesar, the King of Rome.

So in Revelation 12, Satan has seven heads with seven Kings, and [he]{.class_1921} is the eighth King (Rev. 17:10--11). The Devil is the King of a kingdom that has a [mystery]{.class_1921} form, a [religious]{.class_1921} form (Rev. 17:5, 9). But when the Devil becomes incarnate as the Antichrist, three more kingdoms are added to the seven to make the ten Kings of the ten horns (Rev. 13:1). Those three additional kingdoms would be the lion, bear, and leopard in their prophetic fulfillment: England, Russia, and the United States. (Note that only one of those nations is still a monarchy, the leaders of the other two countries ["receive power AS kings"]{.class_1922}---Rev. 17:12. Hitler was definitely a King, even though he did not bear the title.)

So when the Antichrist shows up, he comes with ten Kings who rule with him. He knocks out three of those Kings to become the eighth King (Dan. 7:8, 24). Although I can't say for sure, if I had to guess, I would say the Antichrist gets rid of the last three kingdoms---England, Russia, and America---to set up his kingdom.

So this ["little horn"]{.class_1922} of verse 8 is the Antichrist. It is identified as a man---[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw980.xhtml_page_154}["in this horn were eyes like the eyes of man, and a mouth speaking great things."]{.class_1922} Those ["great things"]{.class_1922} are ["great words against the most High"]{.class_1922} (vs. 25). That is the Antichrist in Revelation 13:6. (We will cover the rest of verse 25 when we get to it.)

9 I beheld till the thrones were cast down, and the Ancient of days did sit, whose garment was white as snow, and the hair of his head like the pure wool: his throne was like the fiery flame, and his wheels as burning fire.

10 A fiery stream issued and came forth from before him: thousand thousands ministered unto him, and ten thousand times ten thousand stood before him: the judgment was set, and the books were opened.

11 I beheld then because of the voice of the great words which the horn spake: I beheld even till the beast was slain, and his body destroyed, and given to the burning flame.

12 As concerning the rest of the beasts, they had their dominion taken away: yet their lives were prolonged for a season and time.

If you want to know the problem in the Prophets in general, and Daniel in particular, it is that, quite often, there are gaps of time skipped over in the narrative. Take, for instance, verses 8 and 9 here in Daniel 7. The vision skips from the Tribulation to the White Throne Judgment, with no Millennium in between. To further complicate matters, sometimes events are given [out of order.]{.class_1921} For example, the body of the beast is cast into the Lake of Fire in verse 11. [If]{.class_1921} that is a reference to the Antichrist (and we will go into another possibility when we comment on the passage), that takes place at Armageddon (Rev. 19:20)---[before the Millennium.]{.class_1921} Moreover, the Second Advent and Millennial kingdom show up in verses 13--14---[after ]{.class_1921}the White Throne Judgment in verses 9--10 and after Armageddon in verse 11. So sometimes, the Holy Ghost records prophecy [backwards.]{.class_1921}

Do you see now why the Amillennialists, Postmillennialists, and even someone like Marvin Rosenthal ([The Pre-Wrath Rapture of the Church]{.class_1921}[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw980.xhtml_page_155}) get so screwed up? Instead of laying out prophetic events according to a clear passage like Revelation 19--20, they will go to passages like Daniel 7 in the Old Testament. One of the laws of Biblical interpretation ("hermeneutics") is always interpret an unclear passage by a clear one, not vice versa.

Now, verses 9--10 are obviously the White Throne Judgment. You can know that for certain because of ["the books"]{.class_1922} that are ["opened"]{.class_1922} in verse 10. That doesn't take place at the Advent (Rev. 19) or at the Judgment of the Nations (Matt. 25); it's at the White Throne Judgment (Rev. 20:12).

["I beheld till the thrones were cast down"]{.class_1922} (vs. 9). You might be able to make that the Second Advent, but if it is, the narrative skips immediately to the White Throne Judgment. Paul lays it out simply and concisely in 1 Corinthians 15:24--26. It is Advent first (1 Cor. 15:24), Millennium second (1 Cor. 15:25), and then the White Throne Judgment (1 Cor. 15:26).

In the context, ["the Ancient of days"]{.class_1922} is a reference to God existing back before Genesis 1:1 (cf. Psa. 102:25). Psalm 90:2 and Habakkuk 1:12 tell you God is ["from everlasting"]{.class_1922}---eternity past. That goes for God the Son just as much as God the Father (Mic. 5:2). That is important to note, because John 5:22; Acts 17:31; and Romans 2:16 make it clear that at the White Throne Judgment, God judges men [by Jesus Christ.]{.class_1921} So although a distinction is made between ["the Son of man"]{.class_1922} and ["the Ancient of days"]{.class_1922} in verse 13, the description of ["the Ancient of days"]{.class_1922} in verses 9--10 here in Daniel 7 matches that of Jesus Christ in Revelation 1:14. So just as ["God was in Christ, reconciling the world unto himself"]{.class_1922} (2 Cor. 5:19), when it comes time for those who have rejected that reconciliation to be judged, God is in Christ judging those sinners.

The ["throne"]{.class_1922} of verse 9 is described in Ezekiel 1, which see. In that chapter, you have a picture of the Second Advent, but that is not the case here in verse 9. But what you should take note of is that in preparation for the White Throne Judgment, the heavens and earth are burned up (2 Pet. 3:10--12 cf. Rev. 20:11). That's called ["the day of the Lord"]{.class_1922} in 2 Peter 3:10 just as the Second Advent is (Joel 1:15, 2:1, 11, 31, 3:14). That is what is going on with that ["fiery stream"]{.class_1922} going out from God in Daniel 7:10---it's burning up the []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw980.xhtml_page_156}creation.

Notice, in verse 10, the two classes of people at this judgment. One group ministers to the Lord. Those are saved Christians who join their Saviour in judging the world (1 Cor. 6:2) and the fallen angels they replaced as ["the sons of God"]{.class_1922} (1 Cor. 6:3 cf. Gen. 6:1--4; Jude 6; John 1:12). The other group is the larger of the two: they are ["ten thousand times ten thousand"]{.class_1922} who stand before the Judge for "final disposition." They died in their sins without Christ (John 3:18, 36); they appear at this judgment to receive their "sentence."

Now Christian, if you want motivation for witnessing, let that be it. One day, you will be sitting behind Christ as a judge. If your momma and daddy were unsaved, you will judge them. If your children were unsaved, you'll be judging them. If your spouse were lost, you will judge him or her. If your neighbors didn't accept Jesus Christ as Saviour, you'll sit in judgment on them. Can you imagine giving your voice against them, [having never told them about Jesus Christ?]{.class_1921}

The Lord told Ezekiel, ["When I say unto the wicked, Thou shalt surely die; and thou givest him not warning, nor speakest to warn the wicked from his wicked way, to save his life; the same wicked man shall die in his iniquity; but his blood will I require at thine hand"]{.class_1922} (Ezek. 3:18).

Paul kept that in mind when he witnessed (Acts 20:26), and did not hesitate to lay the bloodguilt on those who rejected the Gospel (Acts 18:6). He didn't want anyone with whom he had contact to point to him at the judgment and say, "You never told me."

Charles Haddon Spurgeon's mother used to pray for him to get saved, and she would tell the Lord, "I want these prayers to be a witness against him in the day of judgment if he does not get saved." If you have a momma praying for you like that, you will have some sleepless nights, I kid you not.

Now as I said in the introductory remarks on this passage, verse 11 could be a reference to the Antichrist being cast into the lake of fire at the Second Advent, but of course, that is not the context. The context is the White Throne Judgment. In that case, ["the beast,"]{.class_1922} here, would be the Devil himself. That is when Satan will be cast into the Lake of Fire (Rev. 20:10). Of course, Daniel could be seeing the Antichrist and the Devil right together. In that case, []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw980.xhtml_page_157}["the great words"]{.class_1922} of verse 11 would not only be the ["great words against the most High"]{.class_1922} spoken by the Antichrist during the Tribulation (vs. 25), they would be the words the Devil brings as the "prosecuting attorney" at the White Throne Judgment. It will be quite a shock to a lot of people to have their "daddy" (John 8:44), whom they served faithfully their entire life (Eph. 2:2), stand up and speak against them and ask for the "maximum sentence" against them. My, my, my, that will be some day, won't it?

Back to Daniel 7:[ "As concerning the rest of the beasts, they had their dominion taken away: yet their lives were prolonged for a season and time."]{.class_1922} Now we are back to the other three beasts in the chapter: the lion, the bear, and the leopard---England, Russia, and the United States. When Christ returns, those nations are allowed to continue into the Millennium, but they have no ["dominion"]{.class_1922}; that is, no sovereignty or control over their territories. They are what is known as "vassal States," subject to the will of a Judean King in Jerusalem (Zech. 14:9, 16--21).

13 I saw in the night visions, and, behold, one like the Son of man came with the clouds of heaven, and came to the Ancient of days, and they brought him near before him.

14 And there was given him dominion, and glory, and a kingdom, that all people, nations, and languages, should serve him: his dominion is an everlasting dominion, which shall not pass away, and his kingdom that which shall not be destroyed.

The verses obviously refer to the kingdom Christ gets at the Second Advent (Matt. 24:30, 26:64; Rev. 1:7, 14:14--20), but it is not clear whether verse 13 is looking back to the Advent or to something that takes place after the White Throne Judgment. You see, once the Father hands ["The kingdoms of this world"]{.class_1922} over to His Son, that ["reign"]{.class_1922} goes on ["for ever and ever"]{.class_1922} (Rev. 11:15), even after ["when he shall have delivered up the kingdom to God, even the Father"]{.class_1922} (1 Cor. 15:24).

What we have learned here in the book of Daniel is that []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw980.xhtml_page_158}["The kingdoms of this world"]{.class_1922} belong to ["the most High"]{.class_1922}---God the Father---and He gives them ["to whomsoever he will"]{.class_1922} (Dan. 4:17, 25, 32, 5:21). [Right now, ]{.class_1921}He allows the Devil to run them as ["the god of this world"]{.class_1922} (Luke 4:6; 2 Cor. 4:4). But once God is through with Satan, the One to whom He deems to give ["The kingdoms of this world"]{.class_1922} is [His Son.]{.class_1921}

Jesus Christ takes them by right of conquest at Armageddon and rules over them a thousand years. At the end of that thousand years, there is an attempt of the Devil to destroy that reign, but God sends down fire from Heaven and burns up not only the rebellion, but the whole creation (Rev. 20:7--9 cf. 2 Pet. 3:10--12). Then the White Throne Judgment takes place, and the Father, for His own glory, has everyone ["in heaven," "in earth,"]{.class_1922} and ["under the earth"]{.class_1922} (Hell!) bow to His Son and confess Him as Lord (Phil. 2:10--11). If you are lost, the last thing you will do before being cast into the Lake of Fire is admit the One you ignored and rejected is the [One in charge of you]{.class_1921}. Once ["death and hell"]{.class_1922} have been ["cast into the lake of fire"]{.class_1922} (Rev. 20:14), Jesus Christ delivers ["the kingdom"]{.class_1922} to His Father (1 Cor. 15:24--26), who, in return, gives it right back to His Son (Dan. 7:13--14). And as the song goes: ["and he shall reign for ever and ever"]{.class_1922} (Rev. 11:15).

["Of the increase of his government and peace there shall be NO END, upon the THRONE OF DAVID]{.class_1922} \[the throne of a literal, visible, physical kingdom; not some "spiritual" reign\][, and upon his kingdom, to order it, and to establish it with judgment and with justice from henceforth even FOR EVER. The zeal of the LORD of hosts will perform this"]{.class_1922} (Isa. 9:7).

If you want to see this illustrated in type, turn over to Genesis 1. Look at verse 5 there---["And the evening and the morning were the first day."]{.class_1922} Verse 8---["And the evening and the morning were the second day."]{.class_1922} Verse 13---["And the evening and the morning were the third day."]{.class_1922} Verse 19---["And the evening and the morning were the fourth day."]{.class_1922} Verse 23---["And the evening and the morning were the fifth day."]{.class_1922} Verse 31---["And the evening and the morning were the sixth []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw980.xhtml_page_159}day."]{.class_1922}

What about ["the seventh day"]{.class_1922}? God ["rested"]{.class_1922} then. He ["blessed"]{.class_1922} it, He ["sanctified it"]{.class_1922} (Gen. 2:2--3), but there is no evening and morning connected with it. That Sabbath of rest starts and [never ends.]{.class_1921} Whoever wrote that Book told mankind what was going to happen 7,000 years ahead of time. Mohammed and the [Koran]{.class_1921} couldn't touch it.

Verse 14 is the literal fulfillment of the ending of the Disciples' Prayer (incorrectly called the "Lord's Prayer"; it is no prayer the Lord ever prayed [for Himself]{.class_1921} a day in His life) in Matthew 6:13. That is why all the modern "Bibles" remove it. Someone doesn't want Jesus Christ getting ["the kingdom, and the power, and the glory, for ever"]{.class_1922}; they want it for [themselves.]{.class_1921} But when the kingdom finally comes, no Catholic, Moslem, Communist, international Socialist, or coalition of Christians will be responsible for bringing it in. The King will bring in the kingdom, and all the ["dominion, and glory"]{.class_1922} (vs. 14) will go to [Him.]{.class_1921}

15 I Daniel was grieved in my spirit in the midst of my body, and the visions of my head troubled me.

16 I came near unto one of them that stood by, and asked him the truth of all this. So he told me, and made me know the interpretation of the things.

17 These great beasts, which are four, are four kings, which shall arise out of the earth.

18 But the saints of the most High shall take the kingdom, and possess the kingdom for ever, even for ever and ever.

Daniel was ["grieved"]{.class_1922} and ["troubled"]{.class_1922} by what he saw (vs. 15). I imagine he was. If you dreamed about monsters and the Devil incarnate and people going to Hell, I think you'd be upset too. But what upset Daniel the most was trying to make sense of everything he saw. You have the benefit of completed revelation; he didn't.

["I Daniel was grieved in MY SPIRIT IN THE MIDST OF MY BODY"]{.class_1922} (vs. 15). Adam Clarke has some cogent observations on the spirit of man at this point that are worthy of our attention.

1\. "The human spirit is different from the body." Amen! It is also different from the [soul]{.class_1921} (1 Thess. 5:23).

2\. "It has a proper subsistence independently of the body." Amen! For the believer, the spirit subsists on the word of God and prayer, and can experience a renewal which the body cannot (2 Cor. 4:16; Eph. 4:23; Col. 3:10).

3\. "The spirit may exist independently of its body." Stephen's spirit was with his Saviour when his body was dead under a pile of rocks (Acts 7:59).

Verse 16 reveals that there are some people standing by when Daniel has his visions: ["I came near unto one of them that stood by."]{.class_1922} These aren't human beings anymore than the watchers were in chapter 5 or the Princes are in chapter 10. When we get to chapter 8, we will encounter a couple of "saints" speaking to each other who reveal something to Daniel and someone who [appears]{.class_1921} as a man but is an [angel]{.class_1921} (8:15--15 cf. Luke 1:19, 26). Daniel is dealing here with the spirit world; he's receiving truth and interpretation of his visions ["by the disposition of angels"]{.class_1922} (cf. Acts 7:53).

We have already discussed the importance of verse 17 to the interpretation of the vision of the beasts. The beasts not only represent the kingdoms (vs. 23), but the Kings over those kingdoms.

Note the word ["saints"]{.class_1922} in verse 18; the word also shows up in verses 21, 22, 25, and 27 here in Daniel 7. It has no reference to any New Testament Christian. These are the Tribulation Jewish saints with whom the Antichrist makes war (vss. 21, 25 cf. Rev. 13:7). They overcome the Devil by, among other things, not loving their lives to the death (Rev. 12:11). ["The death,"]{.class_1922} in their case, is one specific type of death: beheading (Rev. 20:4). They are rewarded for their faithfulness with a reign with Jesus Christ (Rev. 20:4). That is what is going on in verse 18, as well as verses 22 and 27, here in Daniel 7.

19 Then I would know the truth of the fourth beast, which was diverse from all the others, exceeding dreadful, whose teeth were of iron, and his nails of brass; which devoured, brake in pieces, and stamped the residue with his feet;

20 And of the ten horns that were in his head, and of the []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw980.xhtml_page_161}other which came up, and before whom three fell; even of that horn that had eyes, and a mouth that spake very great things, whose look was more stout than his fellows.

21 I beheld, and the same horn made war with the saints, and prevailed against them;

22 Until the Ancient of days came, and judgment was given to the saints of the most High; and the time came that the saints possessed the kingdom.

23 Thus he said, The fourth beast shall be the fourth kingdom upon earth, which shall be diverse from all kingdoms, and shall devour the whole earth, and shall tread it down, and break it in pieces.

24 And the ten horns out of this kingdom are ten kings that shall arise: and another shall rise after them; and he shall be diverse from the first, and he shall subdue three kings.

25 And he shall speak great words against the most High, and shall wear out the saints of the most High, and think to change times and laws: and they shall be given into his hand until a time and times and the dividing of time.

26 But the judgment shall sit, and they shall take away his dominion, to consume and to destroy it unto the end.

27 And the kingdom and dominion, and the greatness of the kingdom under the whole heaven, shall be given to the people of the saints of the most High, whose kingdom is an everlasting kingdom, and all dominions shall serve and obey him.

I have chosen a rather large passage on which to comment here, but a lot of the material has already been covered in the explanations of the visions above. Here, I will pick up some of the "odds and ends" I haven't mentioned already.

First of all, look at the end of verse 20:[ "whose look was more STOUT than his fellows."]{.class_1922} That's not a reference to the Antichrist's [girth]{.class_1921} (being [fat]{.class_1921}). The word [stout]{.class_1921} is a Middle English word, from Old French, meaning "brave, fierce, proud." In this []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw980.xhtml_page_162}instance, the latter two definitions are applicable. Daniel 8:23 calls the Antichrist ["a king of fierce countenance"]{.class_1922}; Daniel 11:36 says he is a King who ["shall do according to HIS WILL; and he shall EXALT HIMSELF, and MAGNIFY HIMSELF above every god."]{.class_1922}

Secondly, as I gave you back under my remarks on verse 18, ["the saints"]{.class_1922} of this passage are [Jews]{.class_1921} in the Tribulations (note ["the PEOPLE of the saints"]{.class_1922} in vs. 27---their race and nation). But there is a [spiritual, devotional]{.class_1921} application we can make to the New Testament saint from verses 21 and 25. The Devil's two main tactics against the child of God is to [war]{.class_1921} against him (vs. 21) and to [wear him out]{.class_1921} (vs. 25). Paul makes it clear that the saved are in a spiritual warfare against Satan and his forces (Eph. 6:12); hence, the admonition to ["Put on the whole armour of God, that ye may be able to stand against the wiles of the devil"]{.class_1922} (Eph. 6:11).

But just as effective is the wearing out of the saints. Jesus said ["the cares of this world"]{.class_1922} can cause the believer to become ["unfruitful"]{.class_1922} (Mark 4:19). That's all the little piddly stuff that just wears you to a frazzle. Those are things like the washing machine breaking down, getting the laundry done, driving the kids to the soccer game, fussing with your spouse, rotating the tires, changing the oil---a hundred little things that just aggravate the fire out of you.

That's why I stopped flying years before my health broke down. I used to fly out of Pensacola every other week for something like fifty years. Then when they put through all the "security checks," it wasn't long before I gave the whole thing up. You take off anything with metal, and the detector still beeps. So you have to go through again just to prove you're not carrying a weapon on you. You go through, and some woman tells you to take your belt off. Well, I use my belt to keep my pants on, so I have to go through holding my pants up while they want you to hold your hands up to run the "wand" over you. Then it's not just get rid of any metal on you and take off your belt, but take off your shoes. One time I kicked my shoes off and onto the conveyor belt; the woman didn't like that. It just got too much for me. If I had to go through that rigamarole every other week, I would have done something I regretted, so I stopped. It was wearing me out.

During the Civil War, a Yankee Colonel named Abel Streight was sent to destroy the railroads supplying the Confederate army in Tennessee. On the Confederate side, Nathan Bedford Forrest was sent out to stop him. Forrest pursued Streight for sixteen days, but in the last 72 hours of that pursuit, Forrest wasn't able to get fresh mounts. Forrest's men hadn't eaten the last 24 hours of the pursuit and were falling off their horses and collapsing unconscious along the side of the road in exhaustion. Forrest kept up the pursuit with what men he had left (500) and caught up with Streight's superior force of 1,700 men at Cedar Bluff, Alabama. Of course, Streight's men were just as exhausted, and many of them, when they lay in the prone position with their rifles to face Forrest's attack, fell asleep and could not be wakened. Forrest kept up his pursuit until his enemy was more worn out than he was.

That is the state of Christians in this day and age. They are so worn out from ["the cares of this world"]{.class_1922} that they are asleep spiritually from the exhaustion. That is why I preached like I did: I was giving my congregation a swift kick, spiritually, to [wake them up.]{.class_1921} That's why I think Hebrews 12:3 is such a great verse for this age.

"For consider him that endured such contradiction of sinners against himself, lest ye be wearied and faint in your minds."

About the time you want to lay down and quit, consider through what your Saviour went. He went through worse than you are likely to experience, and He didn't quit. Well, if He didn't quit, you don't have to either. Forrest's men were just as exhausted as Streight's men, but Forrest kept going. That's why he won the battle. In a boxing match, the winner is the fighter who can keep going one more round than his opponent. When you feel like quitting, pick yourself up and go one more round.

Notice again, in verse 22, how Jesus Christ is equated with His Father. ["The Ancient of days"]{.class_1922} back up in verse 13 was a reference to God the Father in distinction from ["the Son of man,"]{.class_1922} Jesus Christ. But in verse 22, the reference to ["the Ancient of days"]{.class_1922} coming would have to be to Jesus Christ at the Second Advent. That is when ["judgment was given to the saints"]{.class_1922} and they ["possessed the kingdom"]{.class_1922} (cf. Rev. 20:4).

Next, look down at verse 25. There, the ["great things"]{.class_1922}[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw980.xhtml_page_164} spoken by the ["little horn"]{.class_1922} back up in verse 8 are spoken during the Tribulation period---["time]{.class_1922} \[one year\][ and times ]{.class_1922}\[two years\] [and the dividing of times]{.class_1922} \[a half a year\][."]{.class_1922} That's the length of the Antichrist's reign (Rev. 11:2--3, 12:6, 14, 13:5). So you can see the double application to both the Antichrist and Satan back in verse 8.

Now in verse 25, the Antichrist is characterized by three things:

1\. [Blasphemy]{.class_1921}---["he shall speak great words against the most High."]{.class_1922}

2\. [Persecution]{.class_1921}---["and shall wear out the saints of the most High."]{.class_1922}

3\. [Lawlessness]{.class_1921}---["and think to change times and laws."]{.class_1922}

Note that last one. The Antichrist tries to usurp God's authority on [prophetic matters]{.class_1921} (see 2:21 and our comments on the verse). In other words, when it comes to the ["times,"]{.class_1922} the Antichrist will try to extend his reign and prevent Christ from coming back to establish His kingdom (Rev. 19:19).

The ["laws"]{.class_1922} he will think of changing will be the laws of God in [nature]{.class_1921} and [Scripture.]{.class_1921} You are already seeing that in the generation getting ready to receive the Antichrist. The movement of society these days is to "push the envelope"; that's double-speak for [breaking God's laws.]{.class_1921} It starts with changing the Bible over 323 times (since 1880). Then it goes to removing Bible reading and prayer from the schools (1962--1963). Then it goes to violating every law of art and music (Picasso, Salvador Dali, the Beatles, Aaron Copeland, Andy Warhol, the Rolling Stones, KISS, David Bowie, Alice Cooper, et al.). Then it goes to the "sexual revolution" (fornication and promiscuity) and legalizing of pornography (Miller vs. California, 1973). Then it goes to nudity and sex acts on television ("cable"). Then it's introduce the funny faggot characters, introduce the "caring, sharing" Lesbian talk show hosts, and let the crossdressers come to class with their panties, hose, and make-up. Finally, you legalize two men or two women shacking up together and call it "marriage," and you let the men in the women's bathrooms as long as they "think" they're women. The latest is "transhumanism," where you mess with the genes and mix animals with men and men with machines. You are right back in Genesis 6 in 2353 B.C. How's that for []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw980.xhtml_page_165}your "evolutionary progress"?

["And they shall be given into his hand until a time and times and the dividing of time."]{.class_1922} The ["they"]{.class_1922} could be either ["the saints of the most High"]{.class_1922} or the ["times and laws."]{.class_1922} Both are true for the three-and-a-half years of the Antichrist's "ministry" (Rev. 13:7, 12--15). The promise is, though, at the end of that time, the Antichrist will get what's coming to him: ["But the judgment shall sit, and they shall take away his dominion, to consume and to destroy it unto the end"]{.class_1922} (vs. 26).

Revelation 13:10 says, ["He that leadeth into captivity shall go into captivity: he that killeth with the sword must be killed with the sword. Here is the patience and the faith of the saints."]{.class_1922} In other words, when Christ returns, the Antichrist will get what he's been dishing out for three-and-a-half years. That ["captivity"]{.class_1922} and that ["sword"]{.class_1922} are found in Revelation 19:20--21.

Now the only antecedent in the context for the ["they"]{.class_1922} of verse 26 that makes any sense is ["the saints of the most High"]{.class_1922} in verse 25. Verses 26--27 are the fulfillment of verse 18. Of course, we know that when the Antichrist's ["dominion"]{.class_1922} is taken away, there are more ["saints"]{.class_1922} involved than just Tribulation Jewish saints. Revelation 19:14 says ["the armies which were in heaven"]{.class_1922} accompany Christ at His Advent. Song of Solomon 6:13 tells you there will be ["two armies."]{.class_1922} One of them will be the Body and Bride of Christ on ["white horses"]{.class_1922} (Rev. 19:14), and the other will be the Jewish saints from the Gospels and the Tribulation on ["white asses"]{.class_1922} (see Judg. 5:10 and our comments on that verse in the [Bible Believer's Commentary on Judges and Ruth]{.class_1921}).

["And the kingdom and dominion, and the greatness of the kingdom under the whole heaven, shall be given to the people of the saints of the most High"]{.class_1922} (vs. 27). Like it or not, the day is coming when this whole world will be run by [Jews.]{.class_1921} The Gentiles will exist to serve and nurture that [Jew]{.class_1921} (Isa. 49:22--23, 60:10--11, 16, 61:20). And if a Gentile wants to come to God in that day, he will have to come through a [Jew]{.class_1921} (Zech. 8:23; Isa. 2:2--3).

28 Hitherto is the end of the matter. As for me Daniel, my cogitations much troubled me, and my countenance []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw980.xhtml_page_166}changed in me: but I kept the matter in my heart.

Notice, once more, the expression ["the end"]{.class_1922} in verses 26 and 28. This is the theme of the book of Daniel: the end times (see our comments on 1:15). ["The end of the matter,"]{.class_1922} when it comes to the Book, is the Devil, his King, and his children in the Lake of Fire, Jesus Christ on the throne, and the Jews in charge of the earth (Rom. 4:13).

The word ["cogitations"]{.class_1922} in verse 28 is another word for Daniel's [contemplations]{.class_1921} and [thoughts.]{.class_1921} Daniel is thinking on everything he has seen in these visions, and it's troubling to him (see vs. 15 and comments). In fact, he thinks so seriously on this matter that his ["countenance changed."]{.class_1922} He was so upset by these visions that it manifested on his face. In the next chapter, he has another vision that makes him sick (8:27). That's because he doesn't understand what he's been shown, even though he thinks on it constantly. He keeps everything he saw to himself as Mary did concerning the things about Jesus (Luke 2:19, 51).

Those Old Testament prophets didn't understand everything they wrote or spoke under the inspiration of the Holy Ghost (1 Pet. 1:11). They would write something like Isaiah 53 or Psalm 22 or Genesis 49, and then sit back and stare at what they just wrote and ask God, "What in the ever-lovin', blue-eyed world is that all about?"

In Daniel's case, he "worried himself sick" over what he wrote until the Angel of the Lord showed up and showed him ["that which is noted in the scripture of truth"]{.class_1922} (10:21). If you are ever going to understand that Book, it will be because ["the Spirit of Christ"]{.class_1922} (Rom. 8:9) opens your understanding that you ["might understand the scriptures"]{.class_1922} (Luke 24:45); not through a knowledge of the original languages or a Seminary education. If you want to understand what's in that Book, go to the Author and [ask Him]{.class_1921} for the meaning.

["Open thou mine eyes, that I may behold wondrous things out of thy law"]{.class_1922} (Psa. 119:18).

[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1096.xhtml}

# Chapter 8 {.heading_67-0}

8:1 In the third year of the reign of king Belshazzar a vision appeared unto me, even unto me Daniel, after that which appeared unto me at the first.

2 And I saw in a vision; and it came to pass, when I saw, that I was at Shushan in the palace, which is in the province of Elam; and I saw in a vision, and I was by the river of Ulai.

This is the second of two visions Daniel has during the reign of the last King of Babylon, Belshazzar. The first took place during Belshazzar's first year (see 7:1 and our comments). This second one takes place in Belshazzar's third year (vs. 1). And just as the vision of Daniel 7 was about kingdoms that arose [after]{.class_1921} Belshazzar (see 7:17), this vision also covers two kingdoms that arise after Belshazzar (vss. 20--21). Of course, there [may]{.class_1921} be a future application for us to two kingdoms that will pop up in the next few years, but we will discuss that possibility as we work our way through the chapter.

With verse 1, the language of the book returns to Hebrew. Undoubtedly, the reason is that from verse 1 of chapter 8 to the end of the book, the Lord is dealing with Israel as a nation again, back in the land, with the temple and sacrifices back in operation (see vss. 11--12).

Right away, you know something is different. Shushan in Elam was the capital of the Medo-Persian Empire, not Babylon. No Chaldean monarch had a palace in Shushan; that was the Persians (Neh. 1:1; Esth. 1:2, 5, 2:3, 5, 8, 3:15, etc.). So as the vision starts out, the gold head is gone, just as it was in chapter 7. The vision, like the one in chapter 7, starts in the silver chest: Media-Persia.

["The river of Ulai"]{.class_1922} (vs. 1) has been identified as the Kerkhan River by the scholars; the Greeks called it the "Eulaus." What we know for certain is that it was a river in Elam (what would later be known as Persia), not Babylonia or Chaldea.

3 Then I lifted up mine eyes, and saw, and, behold, there []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1096.xhtml_page_168}stood before the river a ram which had two horns: and the two horns were high; but one was higher than the other, and the higher came up last.

4 I saw the ram pushing westward, and northward, and southward; so that no beasts might stand before him, neither was there any that could deliver out of his hand; but he did according to his will, and became great.

5 And as I was considering, behold, an he goat came from the west on the face of the whole earth, and touched not the ground: and the goat had a notable horn between his eyes.

6 And he came to the ram that had two horns, which I had seen standing before the river, and ran unto him in the fury of his power.

7 And I saw him come close unto the ram, and he was moved with choler against him, and smote the ram, and brake his two horns: and there was no power in the ram to stand before him, but he cast him down to the ground, and stamped upon him: and there was none that could deliver the ram out of his hand.

8 Therefore the he goat waxed very great: and when he was strong, the great horn was broken; and for it came up four notable ones toward the four winds of heaven.

Once more the Gentile kingdoms are represented as [beasts,]{.class_1921} as in chapter 7. This time, the beasts are a two-horned ram and a one-horned goat---a [unicorn.]{.class_1921} The Bible has been mocked for years for its supposedly "mythical creatures," like dragons, satyrs, and unicorns. Now before dismissing the Bible because some scholar thinks the [AV]{.class_1921} translators were referring to the mystical one-horned horse of medieval legend, let us consider the following facts. The scholars who dismiss the translation ["unicorn"]{.class_1922} in Numbers 23:22, 24:8; Job 39:9--10; and Psalm 29:6, 92:10 as an "erroneous translation" of the Hebrew word [re'em]{.class_1921} aren't squeamish at all about accepting [Uintatherium,]{.class_1921} a rhino with [six ]{.class_1921}horns on its head, or [Bramatherium,]{.class_1921} a giraffe with [four]{.class_1921} horns on its head, or [Ceratogaulus,]{.class_1921} a gopher with [two ]{.class_1921}horns on its head, and of course, good old [Triceratops,]{.class_1921} a giant lizard with [three]{.class_1921}[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1096.xhtml_page_169} horns on its head.

You say, "But fossils have been found of those creatures; no one has found a unicorn skeleton." Oh, I don't know about that. Did you know that modern scientists include rhinoceroses (rhinoceri?) in the same order as [horses, asses,]{.class_1921} and [zebras.]{.class_1921} Why be surprised if ancient man did the same thing? There certainly [are]{.class_1921} rhinos with one horn (and that's all the word [unicorn]{.class_1921} means).

I am looking at a picture here with six skulls of ancient, extinct rhinoceroses, and every one of them has [one horn.]{.class_1921} In fact, here is a creature called ["Elasmotherium sibiricum"]{.class_1921} (that's Latin for "thin-plate beast of Siberia"; ain't education the "bee's knees"), commonly known as the "Siberian [unicorn."]{.class_1921} According to the scientists who reject Genesis 1--8, it lived in Eurasia during the Ice Age. They used to think it lived 350,000 years ago, but now they believe it lived 29,000 years ago with man.

I'll do you one better than that. It lived 6,000 years ago with man (Gen. 1:24--31). In fact, it lived 4,000 years ago with man in the Middle East (Gen. 8:1--7). Such a creature certainly would fit the description of Numbers 23:22, 24 and Job 39:9--10. Nothing like a Bible to clear up a "Golden Book of Science."

You say, "But they went extinct before the time of Moses." Oh, I don't know about that either. Here is a 1993 Associated Press news release from Hanoi, Vietnam. A dozen [one-horned]{.class_1921} Java rhinos were found, although the species was thought to have been wiped out. Herds of 35--60 have been confirmed here in the Twenty-first Century.

In his book [Lore of the Unicorn,]{.class_1921} Odell Shephard lists several eyewitness accounts of unicorns. They may not have been the one-horned horses of myth, but they certainly were one-horned creatures that were well-documented. In 1503, Ludovico Barthema, an Italian traveler, actually saw two unicorns in Mecca; the creatures had been given to the Sultan of the city by the King of Ethiopia. Job Ludolphus discusses them in his 1682 [The New History of Ethiopia.]{.class_1921} A Captain Samuel Turner records a conversation he had in 1801 with the rajah of Bhutan (northern India), who claimed to own a unicorn. The December 22, 1860 issue of [The Anthenaeum,]{.class_1921} in reviewing the book [The Romance of Natural History,]{.class_1921}[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1096.xhtml_page_170} said, "The unicorn cannot be pronounced a fable." The missionary-explorer of Africa, David Livingstone (1813--1873), believed in them; and Dr. William Baikie, a scientist who traveled throughout Africa, writes about them in the August 16, 1862 entry in his personal journal. Evidently, the [KJV]{.class_1921} translators of 1611 had more sense than the ignorant, superstitious modern counterparts of the Athenians (see Acts 17:22--23). When the [AV]{.class_1921} 1611 Holy Bible says one thing and modern, educated, "scientific" scholars say something else, never hesitate a moment to deposit the opinions of the scholars where they belong---"File 13."

What you have here is a one-horned goat. So do you know what you had back in 1980? [A neo-pagan]{.class_1921} couple in California creating[ unicorn goats]{.class_1921} by fixing the horn buds on the heads of young Angoran goats so that they grew into a single horn. As we will see in chapter 10, the one-horned goat of Daniel 8 has a [demonic power]{.class_1921} behind it (8:21 cf. 10:20).

Now, God gives us the interpretation of the vision right in the chapter, just as He did in chapters 2 and 7. And just as I did in those two chapters, I am including a chart to illustrate the dream and its interpretation.

[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1122.xhtml}

::: {}
![](image_1129.jpg){.class_979}
:::

[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1130.xhtml}

The ["ram which had two horns"]{.class_1922}[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1130.xhtml_page_172} (vs. 3), which was at a river by the capital of the Persian Empire, had one horn ["higher than the other, and the higher came up last."]{.class_1922} In this case, the beasts are the [kingdoms,]{.class_1921} and the horns are the [Kings.]{.class_1921} Verse 20 tells you the ["two horns are the kings of Media and Persia."]{.class_1922} The smaller of the two horns which came up first would be Darius the Mede from chapter 6; the second and higher horn would be Cyrus the Persian.

So Persia is over east of Babylon pushing westward toward Babylon and Palestine, northward toward Asia Minor and Greece, and southward toward Egypt. And of course, the reason that ["neither was there any that could deliver out of his hand"]{.class_1922} was because [God]{.class_1921} was giving all those lands into the hands of the Kings of Media and Persia. When the Lord defends a city or nation, that city or nation can't be taken, even when faced with a superior force (see 2 Kings 19:32--35). Contrariwise, when the Lord turns a city or nation over to a foreign power, "that's all she wrote" (see Jer. 20:4, 21:10, 34:2; Ezek. 30:25).

God had a controversy with His own people, so He called in Nebuchadnezzar to take them captive (Jer. 25:9). When God was through with Babylon, He called in Cyrus to wipe them out (Isa. 45:1). When He was through with Persia, He called in Alexander the Great. When He got through with the Greeks, He called in Caesar. When finished with Rome, He called in the Ostrogoths, Visigoths, Huns, etc. And on and on through history.

God allows Kings and kingdoms to rise up. As long as they suit His purpose, they exist; and the moment the Lord is through with them, they are cast on the dump heap of history. In the last century, we saw it with England, Germany, and Russia. You are in the process of watching it happen to [America.]{.class_1921} You are now seeing the greatest, most powerful "superpower" the world has ever known, being brought to its knees for setting itself against God's Book.

["But he did according to his will, and became great."]{.class_1922} So despite the fact that [personally]{.class_1921} Darius and Cyrus [may]{.class_1921} have been "saved" in the Old Testament Gentile sense (see Dan. 6:25--27; Ezra 1:2--3), they are still pictures of the [Antichrist.]{.class_1921}

Daniel 11:36---["And the king shall do ACCORDING TO HIS []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1130.xhtml_page_173}WILL; and he shall exalt himself, and magnify himself above every god, and shall speak marvellous things against the God of gods, and shall prosper till the indignation be accomplished: for that that is determined shall be done."]{.class_1922}

So this ram with two horns is pushing from the east, and it seems there is no stopping him. Then in Daniel's vision, ["an he goat"]{.class_1922} comes ["from the west"]{.class_1922} with ["a notable horn between his eyes"]{.class_1922} (vs. 5). The ["he goat"]{.class_1922} is ["the king of Grecia,"]{.class_1922} and the ["notable horn"]{.class_1922} is ["the first king"]{.class_1922} of that kingdom (vs. 21). That would be Alexander the Great, who defeated Darius III at the Battle of Gaugamela in 331 B.C.

["And touched not the ground"]{.class_1922} (vs. 5); ["ran upon him in the fury of his power"]{.class_1922} (vs. 6). The military strategy of ["Blitzkrieg"]{.class_1921} ("lightning war") was not new to the Germans in World War II; Alexander the Great utilized it in his battles. Within a period of only three years (334--331 B.C.), Alexander had conquered the greatest army of that time, the Persians. He went up against a force over twice the size (47,000 against 100,000) with only a 2.5% loss in his forces. His army managed a kill rate of nine out of ten: 90%. ["There was no power in the ram to stand before him . . . and there was none that could deliver the ram out of his hand"]{.class_1922} (vs. 7).

The word ["choler"]{.class_1922} in verse 7 is another word for ["the fury"]{.class_1922} of verse 6. It means "anger." We get the word [cholera]{.class_1921} from that word.

Now Alexander is one of the few conquerors who moves west to east with success. He starts out conquering Greece and then crosses the Hellespont to take on Persia and, eventually, India. He has the largest empire of the ancient world.

But as we pointed out in Daniel 2, the movement in the Bible is from east to west. When Napoleon and Hitler tried to move west to east and take Russia, they both "lost their shirts." Though successful in his military campaigns, Alexander paid personally for the west-to-east movement. Upon returning to Babylon from his India campaign, he finally succumbed to the ravages of years of alcoholism. After a night of extremely heavy drinking, he took fever and died ten days later at the age of 32 (one month short of his 33rd birthday). ["When he was strong, the great horn was broken"]{.class_1922} (vs. 8). The practical application should be obvious: ["whosoever exalteth himself shall be abased"]{.class_1922}[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1130.xhtml_page_174} (Luke 14:11).

Historically, when Alexander died, his kingdom ended up being split between four of his Generals: Greece and Macedonia went to Cassander; Thrace and most of western Asia Minor went to Lysimachus; Ptolemy got Egypt and Palestine (a point of contention between the Ptolemies and the Seleucids, as we will see in the historical material in chap. 11); and Seleucus got the eastern part of Asia Minor, Mesopotamia, and Persia. Simplified, those regions would be Greece, Asia Minor, Egypt, and Syria. They would match ["the four winds of heaven"]{.class_1922} (vs. 8) by Asia Minor in the [north,]{.class_1921} Egypt in the [south,]{.class_1921} Syria in the [east,]{.class_1921} and Greece in the [west.]{.class_1921} To us, that is history. Of course, to Daniel, it was still prophecy, for he was writing about it nearly 230 years ahead of time.

But as we are about to see, there is still a future application that is prophetic to us. Verse 9 introduces the Antichrist under the symbolism of the ["little horn."]{.class_1922} So in chapter 2, you have [four]{.class_1921} Gentile kingdoms and then the kingdom of the Antichrist. In chapter 7, you have [three]{.class_1921} Gentile kingdoms and then the kingdom of the Antichrist, but those three kingdoms have a [double application.]{.class_1921} They not only represent Persia, Greece, and Rome; they can also apply to Britain, Russia, and the United States.

I believe you have the same situation here. You have [two]{.class_1921} kingdoms and then the kingdom of the Antichrist. Historically (to us), they are Persia and Greece, but I am of the opinion that those two kingdoms also represent two kingdoms that will show up after the Lord has dumped the United States. Right now as of this writing (2015), I am not sure exactly what two kingdoms they could be. The time is so short right now, that the only guess I have to make is that they are two kingdoms that show up either immediately preceding the Rapture or during the time when the Antichrist comes in to peacefully establish his kingdom before all hell breaks loose during the Great Tribulation (see Dan. 11; Rev. 6). If that be the case, that would give you [ten]{.class_1921} kingdoms in the visions of the book of Daniel---the number of the Gentiles.

1\. Babylon.

2\. Medo-Persia.

3\. Greece.

4\. Rome.

5\. England.

6\. Russia.

7\. The United States.

8\. Unknown.

9\. Unknown.

10. The kingdom of the Antichrist.

9 And out of one of them came forth a little horn, which waxed exceeding great, toward the south, and toward the east, and toward the pleasant land.

10 And it waxed great, even to the host of heaven; and it cast down some of the host and of the stars to the ground, and stamped upon them.

11 Yea, he magnified himself even to the prince of the host, and by him the daily sacrifice was taken away, and the place of his sanctuary was cast down.

12 And an host was given him against the daily sacrifice by reason of transgression, and it cast down the truth to the ground; and it practised, and prospered.

13 Then I heard one saint speaking, and another saint said unto that certain saint which spake, How long shall be the vision concerning the daily sacrifice, and the transgression of desolation, to give both the sanctuary and the host to be trodden under foot?

14 And he said unto me, Unto two thousand and three hundred days; then shall the sanctuary be cleansed.

There is no doubt who this ["little horn"]{.class_1922} is; we have already run into him back in 7:8. Of course, if you have a [Scofield Reference Bible,]{.class_1921} that is not the case. In his note on 8:9, Scofield says, "The 'little horn' here is a prophecy FULFILLED IN ANTIOCHUS EPIPHANES, B.C. 175 . . . He is NOT to be confounded with the 'little horn' of Dan. 7 who is yet to come."

Scofield's reasoning is that the ["little horn"]{.class_1922} of Daniel 7 comes out of the Roman Empire, while the ["little horn"]{.class_1922} of Daniel 8 comes out of the Greek Empire. But that is because Scofield, as all the prophetic expositors, ignores the [future]{.class_1921}[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1130.xhtml_page_176} tense of the verb in the latter part of 7:17 (see our comments under 7:1).

While Larkin doesn't have the beasts right in Daniel 7 either, he is still much more careful in his reading of Daniel 8. He takes you down to ["the latter time of their kingdom"]{.class_1922} in the interpretation in verse 23 and points out the fact that Antiochus Epiphanes was a good 145 years away from ["the latter time of their kingdom"]{.class_1922} (Egypt, the last of the four kingdoms, fell to the Romans in 30 B.C.). The ["latter time"]{.class_1922} is obviously a reference to the time immediately preceding the Second Advent (i.e., the Tribulation), as it is everywhere else it shows up in Scripture (Num. 24:14; Ezek. 38:8, 16; Dan. 10:14; 1 Tim. 4:1). Even Scofield can't get away from the fact that, in the interpretation of the vision, verses 24--25 have [nothing]{.class_1921} to do with Antiochus Epiphanes.

So here we have a great truth of Bible prophecy. A prophecy in the Bible can have a [double,]{.class_1921} and sometimes a [triple,]{.class_1921} application, with the final application being the literal fulfillment of the prophecy. There is no doubt that Antiochus Epiphanes and the destruction of Jerusalem by the Romans in A.D. 70 were [types]{.class_1921} of what you read here, but they were certainly not the actual fulfillment of the prophecy, and that is evident by what follows.

What is important to get from verse 9 is that the Antichrist comes from one of the four divisions of Alexander's kingdom: Greece, Asia Minor, Syria, or Egypt. As a matter of fact, Larkin has the three displaced horns of 7:8 being the other three kingdoms of the Greek Empire, which he believes will be part of the Antichrist's ten-kingdom federation. I am not completely sure about that, but the point of verse 9 here in Daniel 8 is that the Antichrist will come (at least ethnically) from either Greece, Turkey, Syria, or Egypt.

I teach he comes from [Syria.]{.class_1921} Now why is that? Well, the only apostle of the original twelve not from Galilee was Judas Iscariot. Jesus Christ identifies him as the Son of Perdition (John 17:12), the title of the Antichrist (2 Thess. 2:3). The word [Iscariot]{.class_1921} means "man of Kerioth." Although there is more than one Kerioth in the Bible, the one associated with the Antichrist is the one in [Moab.]{.class_1921}

["The HORN of Moab]{.class_1922} \[Dan. 7:8, 8:9\][ is cut off, and HIS ARM IS BROKEN]{.class_1922} \[the Antichrist has a [bad arm]{.class_1921}---Zech. 11:17\][, saith the LORD"]{.class_1922}[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1130.xhtml_page_177} (Jer. 48:25).

So I teach the Antichrist is part Syrian from Moab (Jordan in our day), because at the time of Christ, Moab was part of the Roman province of Syria (cf. Luke 2:1--2). We will get into the Antichrist's Jewish connections when we get to 11:38 here in Daniel.

Back to Daniel 8:9---["which waxed exceeding great, toward the south ]{.class_1922}\[Egypt\][, and toward the east]{.class_1922} \[Babylon in the Tribulation---see Zech. 5:9--11 and our comments in that Commentary\][, and toward the pleasant land]{.class_1922} \[Israel---Jer. 3:19; Zech. 7:14\][."]{.class_1922} That is why the Antichrist doesn't come from Egypt, Asia Minor, or Greece. Three directions are given in the verse: ["south," "east,"]{.class_1922} and ["the pleasant land"]{.class_1922} for west. The Antichrist doesn't come from Egypt, because Egypt is the southernmost kingdom; the ["little horn"]{.class_1922} doesn't ["wax great"]{.class_1922} to the north. He doesn't come from Greece or Asia Minor, because ["the pleasant land"]{.class_1922} is south of both of them, and ["the south"]{.class_1922} is given as a different direction than ["the pleasant land."]{.class_1922}

Verse 10---["And it waxed great, even to the host of heaven; and it cast down some of the host and of the stars to the ground."]{.class_1922} Then it's not Antiochus Epiphanies or Titus. This is a [supernatural]{.class_1921} thing. This isn't ["the host of heaven"]{.class_1922} as in the stars and the planets (see Deut. 4:19, 17:3; 2 Kings 23:5). No astronaut or "cosmonaut" can reach them in a rocket ship or starship no matter if he did have "warp drive," "hyperspace," or "wormholes." The ["host of heaven"]{.class_1922} here in verse 10 is the angelic host found in 1 Kings 22:19; 2 Chronicles 18:18; and Revelation 1:20. These are the principalities and powers of Ephesians 6:12 that are drawn out of the third heaven by the Dragon in Revelation 12:3--4, and are said to be the Devil's angels in Revelation 12:9. The ["little horn"]{.class_1922} of Daniel 8 is not Antiochus Epiphanes or any normal, natural man; he is [Satan incarnate.]{.class_1921}

["Yea, he magnified himself even to the prince of the host"]{.class_1922} (vs. 11). ["The prince of the host"]{.class_1922} would be the One in charge of that host back in verse 10, a supernatural host up in the third heaven; that would be ["the Prince of princes"]{.class_1922} down in verse 25---the Lord Jesus Christ (Rev. 17:14, 19:13--16). He is ["the captain of the LORD'S host"]{.class_1922} (Josh. 5:14--15). One of the titles of God throughout the Old Testament is ["the LORD of hosts."]{.class_1922}[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1130.xhtml_page_178} This is the Devil trying to ["exalt ]{.class_1922}\[his\][ throne above the stars of God"]{.class_1922} (Isa. 14:13).

["And by him the daily sacrifice was taken away, and the place of his sanctuary was cast down."]{.class_1922} Whether you realize it or not, there is a lot in that part of verse 11. The first is another proof that the ["little horn"]{.class_1922} in this chapter is NOT Antiochus Epiphanes. You see, when the Antichrist takes ["away the daily sacrifice,"]{.class_1922} he puts ["the abomination that maketh desolate"]{.class_1922} in its place (vs. 12 cf. 11:31). According to the Lord Jesus Christ, that event had not taken place during the intertestamental period (Matt. 24:15; Mark 13:14). And though the Christians in Jerusalem used Christ's warning to flee the city when they saw the Roman eagle on the banners of Titus' armies in A.D. 70, that was still not the fulfillment of the prophecy, for the Lord went on to say:

["For then shall be great tribulation, such as was not since the beginning of the world to this time, no, nor ever shall be" ]{.class_1922}(Matt. 24:21).

There have been troubles and afflictions as great as, and greater than, the destruction of Jerusalem by the Romans. We have listed a few of these in our teaching on Mark 13:19. The taking away of ["the daily sacrifice"]{.class_1937-0} is followed by a period of time so terrible that no event in the history of the world---including the Flood of Noah's day---can compare to it. The world has [never]{.class_1938} known a time like that and won't until the Great Tribulation. Preterists like John Bray don't know about what in the world they are talking.

The second important thing you should note is that ["daily sacrifice."]{.class_1922} That's the ["two lambs of the first year day by day continually,"]{.class_1922} one at morning and the other at evening, commanded by God back in Exodus 29:38--39. Hebrews 10:11 says, ["And every priest standeth daily ministering and offering oftentimes the same sacrifices."]{.class_1922} Well, that's not now; no sacrifice has been offered daily on the altar of any temple since A.D. 70.

The verse is a prophecy of the renewal of the Jewish sacrifice, and for that to happen, the temple will have to be rebuilt. With the modern revival of Calvinism among Conservative Evangelicals, []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1130.xhtml_page_179}there has been a revival of the Amillennialism of Augustine. That is accompanied by "replacement theology" where the Church takes the place of Israel. That means God is all done with the Jews, so people like Texe Marrs and Steve Anderson teach that the Jews don't belong in the land, and they would be sinning to reconstruct the temple since it was done away with by the sacrifice of Jesus Christ (ignoring the prophetic nature of Col. 2:17).

But not only will there be a temple in the Millennium with sacrifices (Ezek. 41--46), there will be one in the Tribulation.

["And there was given me a reed like unto a rod: and the angel stood, saying, Rise, and measure the temple of God, and the altar, and them that worship therein. But the court which is without the temple leave out, and measure it not; for it is given unto the Gentiles: and the holy city shall they tread under foot forty and two months" ]{.class_1922}(Rev. 11:1--2).
