That's future, after A.D. 90. The Temple had been destroyed in A.D. 70, so it's not talking about that. The 42 months of Revelation 11:2 is the time period for the Great Tribulation. The Antichrist enters into a Jewish temple with an altar where a sacrifice is being made daily.

The Jews are prepared to rebuild their temple as soon as God takes down the Moslem mosque on the Temple mount by allowing the Jews to take the Temple mount for themselves and tear down the Dome of the Rock or by sending a natural disaster to destroy it. The only other two options are either to build it in a different spot in Jerusalem (sites have been proposed for the ancient Temple being just north or south of the Mosque of Omar) or by entering into an "ecumenical venture" with the Moslems (see our comments on 11:27). Regardless of [how]{.class_1921} it comes to pass, a Jewish temple [will]{.class_1921} be rebuilt.

Right now in Israel, there is an organization called the "Temple Institute." It has made many of the temple vessels, as well as the priests' garments. It has genetically identified what is believed to be descendants of the tribe of Levi who are being trained as priests, all the way to learning how to properly make animal sacrifices. The head of a group called the "Temple Mount Faithful," named Gershon Salomon, has tried every six months since 1991 to lay a four-ton []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1130.xhtml_page_180}cornerstone to begin the construction of the temple. All the way back in 1967, a British Christian magazine reported that Jewish masons were brought to Bedford, Indiana to study pneumatic drills for stonecutting; the stone they studied cutting was similar to [Jerusalem limestone.]{.class_1921} After that, 500 railroad cars of pre-cut limestone from Bedford, Indiana were sent to Pier 26 in New York where they were shipped to Jerusalem. The stage is set; the orchestra has tuned up. The only thing for which we are waiting is for the conductor to take His place and begin the symphony (Rev. 5:5--9).

Now go back and read Revelation 11:2. The courtyard of the Tribulation temple, where the altar is (see Exod. 40:33; 1 Kings 8:64; 2 Chron. 7:7), isn't measured because ["it is given unto the Gentiles: and the holy city shall they tread under foot forty and two months."]{.class_1922} That's about what you read in Daniel 8:13.

In the Tribulation, over comes "His Majesty" from Rome to Jerusalem. As he is touring around, waving at everybody, making speeches about "peace in our time" and "peace on earth to men of good will" and the "peace process" with the "religion of peace," someone takes a shotgun or something to him like that Turk did to John Paul II back in 1981.

"His Holiness" is assassinated and laid in state for three days and three nights. Then the spirit of Judas Iscariot (John 17:12) comes up from ["his own place"]{.class_1922} (Acts 1:25) in the Pit (Rev. 9:11) and enters the dead body of that Man of Sin, while the soul of the Devil comes down from the third heaven (Rev. 12:9) and brings that dead body back to life (Rev. 13:2--3); and out of that casket comes the Son of Perdition (2 Thess. 2:3), Satan incarnate (2 Thess. 2:7--8). He comes up with a bad right eye and bad arm (Zech. 11:17).

That's when the real horror show begins. As a perfect "imitation" (see the reading of 1 Cor. 11:1 in the modern perversions of the Bible) of the resurrected Christ, the Son of Perdition enters the rebuilt Jewish temple and goes to the Holy of Holies. There, he sits down on the mercy seat of the Ark of the Covenant. He puts one hand on one cherub and his other hand on the other cherub, and says to the TV cameras and to the Jewish priests standing there horror-stricken, "I am God \[2 Thess. 2:4\]; the worship service will now begin."

And it begins. His "bully boys" and thugs go out to the brazen altar there in the courtyard and stop the sacrifice of those two lambs every day. In their place, the Antichrist starts his own sacrifices: Jews beheaded at the altar (Rev. 6:9 cf. Rev. 20:4). Their flesh is eaten (Isa. 6:13), and their blood is drunk (Psa. 16:4) in a "Mass" to ["the god of this world"]{.class_1922} (1 Cor. 10:20--21 cf. 2 Cor. 4:4; Dan. 11:38). To top everything off, the False Prophet has an image of the Antichrist set up, and whoever won't worship it will be killed (Rev. 13:11--15); it's Daniel 3 all over again. That is what is involved ["concerning the daily sacrifice and the transgression of desolation"]{.class_1922} (vs. 13).

Now as night follows day, it should be obvious to anyone that if the temple is rebuilt and the sacrifices are reinstated, that the Mosaic Law is coming back into effect with the departure of the Body of Christ. With the return of the temple and animal sacrifices comes [Moses and Elijah]{.class_1921} (Rev. 11:3--6): [the Law and the Prophets.]{.class_1921} So the last commandment in the Old Testament to that Jew is: ["Remember ye the LAW OF MOSES"]{.class_1922} (Mal. 4:4); NOT ["the gospel of the grace of God"]{.class_1922} (Acts 20:24). So in the Tribulation, salvation is NOT by grace alone through faith alone in the finished work of Jesus Christ. It is ["keep the COMMANDMENTS of God, AND have the testimony of Jesus Christ"]{.class_1922} (Rev. 12:17); it is ["keep the COMMANDMENTS of God, AND the faith of Jesus"]{.class_1922} (Rev. 14:12).

In the Tribulation, the one body of Jews and Gentiles in Jesus Christ (Eph. 4:4, 2:11--16; Gal. 3:28), sealed by the indwelling Holy Spirit (Eph. 1:13, 4:30), is gone from the earth (Rev. 5:9--10), and is replaced by a body of saved Jews (Rev. 7:3--8) that is [separate from]{.class_1921} another body made up of saved Gentiles (Rev. 7:9). The Jews are saved by being ["sealed . . . in their foreheads"]{.class_1922} (Rev. 7:3) because they ["sigh and . . . cry for all the abominations"]{.class_1922} done in Israel and Jerusalem (Ezek. 9:4)---WORKS. The Gentiles are saved by washing their OWN ROBES[ "white in the blood of the Lamb"]{.class_1922} (Rev. 7:14); not by being washed THEMSELVES BY JESUS CHRIST from their ["sins in his own blood"]{.class_1922} (Rev. 1:5).

You say, "What's the difference, Ruckman?" In the New Testament, the [Lord]{.class_1921} does the washing, and He washes [you.]{.class_1921} In the Tribulation, the [Gentile saints]{.class_1921} do the washing, and they wash []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1130.xhtml_page_182}[their own]{.class_1921} [robes]{.class_1921}---not themselves. That's WORKS. I know you won't get that from the major Christian Colleges and Universities, or from any "megachurch," or from J. Vernon McGee as he goes "Through the Bible"; but they don't get much beyond the "fundamentals of the faith," not being "serious students of the Bible."

Verse 12: ["And an host was given him."]{.class_1922} The Devil gets a third of the angels in Revelation 12:4. ["And it]{.class_1922} \[i.e., the [host]{.class_1921}\][ cast down the truth to the ground."]{.class_1922} "Glory, glory, hallelujah; His truth is marching on!"[ No, it ain't;]{.class_1921} it's ["fallen in the street"]{.class_1922} and ["faileth"]{.class_1922} (Isa. 59:14--15). The thing that marks this lost world, especially in the Tribulation, is its [hatred of the truth;]{.class_1921} that's what allows the Devil to take control (2 Thess. 2:8--10). "His truth is marching on" [into the gutter.]{.class_1921} That deluded Unitarian woman who wrote "The Battle Hymn of the Republic" (Julia Ward Howe) was as crazy as a bandicoot.

Now we have discussed the [possibility]{.class_1921} of the two saints being angels back under 4:13 and 7:16 (which see). However, that is not how the word is used in Daniel or throughout the Old Testament. When you hear a Calvinist talk about the "Perseverance of the Saints," you need to remember that the term [saint]{.class_1921} is first an [Old Testament]{.class_1921} term that has been transferred and applied to a New Testament believer. No "saint" in the Old Testament was a "Christian"; no Christians show up in your Bible until Acts 11:26. Before the Law, it is a reference to anyone who believes and follows the one, true God (e.g., Job 5:1, 15:15). Under the Law, it is used of the [Jews]{.class_1921} (Deut. 33:3; 2 Chron. 6:41; Psa. 50:5, 79:2, 85:8, 132:9, 16, 148:14, 149:1; Hos. 11:12). That is the case here in Daniel (see 7:18, 21--22, 25, 27). If these are not angels, I would say that Daniel is seeing into the future like John did in the Revelation, and these two saints talking to him are a couple of those Jews ["slain for the word of God"]{.class_1922} in Revelation 6:9, who are rewarded with a reign in Christ's kingdom in Revelation 20:4.

The question of verse 13 opens up a "can of worms" as far as prophetic "arithmetic" is concerned. You see, [four conflicting dates]{.class_1921} are given in Scripture in connection to Daniel's Seventieth Week and the Great Tribulation. I have included a chart so you can see the []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1130.xhtml_page_183}discrepancies involved.

Daniel 9:27 makes it clear that Daniel's Seventieth Week is a period of seven years divided into two periods of three-and-a-half years each (Dan. 7:25; Rev. 12:14), or 1,260 days each (Rev. 11:3, 12:6), with the last half being called the "Great Tribulation" (Matt. 24:21). If you added both halves of Daniel's Seventieth Week together, that would give you 2,520 days.

Daniel 8:14 gives 2,300 days for the Tribulation. That is an extra 1,040 days added onto one of the halves of Daniel's Seventieth Week. I add those days onto the first 1,260 days, giving a total of 2,300 days total for both halves. Clarence Larkin adds them onto the last 1,260 (from the taking away of the daily sacrifice), going two years, ten months, and twenty days into the Millennium (we will explain his reason why in a moment).

[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1200.xhtml}

Daniel 12:11 records 1,290 days; that's thirty days added to the 1,260. Daniel 12:12 gives 1,335 days; that's an extra 45 days added onto the 1,290 days of the previous verse. Daniel 12:11 would give 2,550 days for both halves of Daniel's Seventieth Week; Daniel 12:12 would give a total of 2,595 days.

Now look at that: four obscure numbers on which the Holy Spirit has given no clear illumination yet. Is that anything on which to build a theology? Of course not! Yet that is exactly on what the Seventh-day Adventists build their convoluted system. William Miller made the 2,300 days "prophetic days" (as in 9:27) and had Christ returning 2,300 years after 457 B.C., in 1843. (Commentators like Adam Clarke don't do much better; they date the 2,300 years from Alexander the Great's invasion of Asia Minor in 334 B.C. That would have put the Second Advent in 1966.) When Christ didn't return in 1843, Miller's followers recalculated and predicted the Second Coming would be the next year (shades of Harold Camping!). And of course, when it didn't happen that year either, they [spiritualized it]{.class_1921} (don't you know!). They had the [temple in Heaven]{.class_1921} (see Rev. 11:19) being the one cleansed in a "Day of Atonement" accomplished in 1814. You couldn't find that in Scripture with a laser beam and a flashlight. In digging through Hebrews to justify an erroneous view of the Second Coming and to get you back under the Old Testament Law, the Millerites overlooked that ["now"]{.class_1922} in Hebrews 9:24. Christ was in the "Holy of Holies" in Glory back in A.D. 64; He didn't suddenly move in there in 1844.

All Scripture is the word of God, but not all Scripture is [foundational.]{.class_1921} You don't build a skyscraper on a foundation of light bulbs, and you don't build a theology on a passage as obscure as Daniel 8:14. It's like a Catholic Pope trying to use Matthew 16:19 for the foundation of his church without knowing what the ["rock"]{.class_1922} is, what the ["church"]{.class_1922} is, or what ["the gates of hell"]{.class_1922} are. You are headed for a spiritual disaster.

The ["days"]{.class_1922} of Daniel 8:14 and 12:11--12 aren't "prophetic days" representing years, as the "days" of Daniel's Seventieth Week which define the length of that week (Rev. 11:3, 12:6). Undoubtedly, the differences in the numbers have to do with when the post-Tribulation rapture, the Advent, and the cleansing of the temple []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1200.xhtml_page_186}occur. Larkin has Daniel 8:14 being the time when the daily sacrifice is stopped to when it is reinstituted in the Millennial Temple. As far as I can see, there is not enough information to make a definitive statement on the matter, so I will just leave it there until the Holy Ghost shows somebody else more than He has shown me.

15 And it came to pass, when I, even I Daniel, had seen the vision, and sought for the meaning, then, behold, there stood before me as the appearance of a man.

16 And I heard a man's voice between the banks of Ulai, which called, and said, Gabriel, make this man to understand the vision.

17 So he came near where I stood: and when he came, I was afraid, and fell upon my face: but he said unto me, Understand, O son of man: for at the time of the end shall be the vision.

18 Now as he was speaking with me, I was in a deep sleep on my face toward the ground: but he touched me, and set me upright.

Again, Daniel seeks for the meaning of what was shown him (see 7:16, 20). Daniel is once more going to the ["God in heaven that revealeth secrets"]{.class_1922} (2:28). There was nothing in Daniel naturally that enabled him to get the interpretation. God had to give it to him, or he wouldn't get it (see Gen. 41:16). God isn't going to give the answer to any man or church that usurps His name, position, and authority (Isa. 42:8).

In response to Daniel's search for the meaning of the vision, God sends Daniel an angel, and there is no doubt this time that it is an angel (see our remarks on the saints of vs. 13). This is the angel Gabriel who appeared to Zacharias and Mary in Luke 1:19, 26. Note that in Luke 1, when Gabriel announces the births of John the Baptist and Jesus Christ, no mention is made by him of the atoning work of Jesus Christ at His First Advent; everything he says has to do with Christ's Second Advent---read Luke 1:13--20, 26--36.

So when Gabriel addresses Daniel, he addresses him as ["son of man"]{.class_1922} (vs. 17). That is what Ezekiel is called throughout his []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1200.xhtml_page_187}prophecy (Ezek. 2:1, 3, 6, 8, 3:1, 3--4, 10, 17, 25, 4:1, 16, 5:1, 6:2, 7:2, 8:5--6, 8, 12, 15, 17, etc.). That is what Christ is called at His Second Advent (Matt. 24:27, 30, 37, 44, 26:64; Mark 13:26, 14:62; Luke 17:26, 30, 22:69; Acts 7:56). Both Ezekiel and Daniel are types of Tribulation saints who witness to Gentiles, and both see appearances of Christ in His glory (Ezek. 1; Dan. 10).

Also, look at what Gabriel says to Daniel in verse 17: ["Understand, O son of man: for at the TIME OF THE END shall be the vision."]{.class_1922} Look again at verse 19: ["Behold, I will make thee know what shall be in the LAST END of the indignation: for at the time appointed THE END shall be." "The end"]{.class_1922}---the time immediately preceding the Second Advent (see our comments on 1:15). This is why I believe there is a [future]{.class_1921} application to the ram and the he goat; the interpretation applies to ["the end,"]{.class_1922} not just the silver chest and brass loins of Nebuchadnezzar's image.

Before moving on to the next passage, I want you to notice two things about angels in general and Gabriel in particular. First, note that Gabriel is said to appear as ["a MAN"]{.class_1922} (vs. 15). In the Bible, all angels are [male]{.class_1921} (see Judg. 13:3, 6, 8--9, 10--11; Rev. 21:17); there is not a female angel in that Book. Ladies, I hate to tell you, but if you are going to be ["as the angels of God in heaven"]{.class_1922} someday (Matt. 22:30), you are going to be [male;]{.class_1921} that's why you are called a [son of God]{.class_1921} positionally (1 John 3:1--2), even though you may be one of God's daughters practically this side of the Rapture (2 Cor. 6:18). Everywhere in that Book where angels show up, they appear as [men]{.class_1921} with [no wings.]{.class_1921}

Some of the brethren (who wouldn't have any "ministry" at all if it weren't for "Ruckman") get onto me because of my teaching on angels. They will say that I have to deny cherubim and seraphim are angels. I don't have to "deny" anything. Get out your concordance or a computer Bible and look up the words; they aren't called "angels" anywhere in that Book.

Those birds will say, "Well, Ruckman teaches angels are 33½-year-old males with no Scripture to back it up"; then they will cite [one page]{.class_1921} of my work on "Angelology" in [Theological Studies,]{.class_1921} Vol. I (pg. 964, 1998 ed.). Being too lazy or too crooked to look across the []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1200.xhtml_page_188}page to page 965, they miss all the following material.

1\. Every angel in the Book is [male]{.class_1921} with [no wings]{.class_1921} (Judg. 13--15; Luke 24; Rev. 21--22).

2\. Jesus Christ is called ["the angel of God"]{.class_1922} (Acts 27:23; Gal. 4:14) before and after His resurrection (see also our comments on Hos. 12:3--4 in the [Bible Believer's Commentary on the Minor Prophets, ]{.class_1921}Vol. I). He is also [the]{.class_1921} Son of God,[ ]{.class_1921}while the angels are ["SONS of God"]{.class_1922}[ ]{.class_1921}(Job 38:7).

3\. In His resurrection body, Jesus Christ is a 33½-year-old male (Luke 3:23 cf. John 2:23, 5:1, 6:4, 13:1).

4\. ["The children of the resurrection,"]{.class_1922} who ["are the children of God"]{.class_1922} (cf. Rom. 8:16, 21), are ["as the angels of God in heaven"]{.class_1922} (Matt. 22:30) and are ["equal"]{.class_1922} to them (Luke 20:36). Well, what are ["the children of the resurrection"]{.class_1922} like when they come up? They are like their Saviour (1 John 3:2), who was a [33½-year-old male at His resurrection.]{.class_1921} That means if they are ["equal unto the angels"]{.class_1922} (Luke 20:36), then those angels are [33½-year-old men.]{.class_1921}

That's Ruckman's no "Scripture reference to prove it." These birds depend on the laziness and gullibility of their readers. They like to make shocking statements that elicit an "I can't believe anyone would say such a thing!" response from their readers, without ever discussing what the Scriptures say on the matter.

Take the charge "Ruckman teaches that angels are stars." My stars! What heresy! Why would "Ruckman" make such an outlandish claim?! I gave three references in Revelation (Rev. 12:4, 9, 9:1), and not one is discussed. Angels aren't just "sometimes symbolized by stars in Revelation," they are called ["stars"]{.class_1922} before Genesis 1:1 (Job 38:4--7).

And of course, they don't like me teaching that no angel in the Bible has wings; after all they fly, don't they (Dan. 9:21; Rev. 14:6)? Superman, Captain Marvel, Wonder Woman, and dozens of other "super heroes" have been flying around in the funny books for over eighty years; none except a few (like Flash Gordon's "hawkmen") have wings. What makes you think a supernatural being empowered by God Almighty (see our remarks under 9:21) has to have wings to fly?

The response to that is, "Well, Ruckman, don't you draw wings on angels?" Of course I do, because if I didn't, the average person would say, "What's that?" The average American (even the Christian) doesn't know what the Bible says about angels; all he knows are the angels of Roman Catholic fiction. I put wings on them, even though I know angels don't have them (and I often tell my audience so), so my congregation will know what they are.

I use several "images" in my chalk talks and art that convey a certain idea to the viewers. I use the "star of David" to illustrate Israel. Well, the star of David is not a Bible symbol of Israel; it comes from pagan idolatry (Acts 7:43). But it is readily associated with Israel, so I use it. Evidently these inexperienced children have a hard time distinguishing between [teaching the Bible doctrinally]{.class_1921} and [illustrating it practically.]{.class_1921}

The second thing you need to notice is how Gabriel spoke to Daniel and how Daniel reacted to Gabriel. Daniel ["was afraid, and fell upon]{.class_1922} \[his\][ face"]{.class_1922} (vs. 17). Gabriel ["touched]{.class_1922} \[him\][, and set ]{.class_1922}\[him\][ upright"]{.class_1922} (vs. 18). What Gabriel did NOT do was [strangle]{.class_1921} Daniel.

You say, "Why do you say that, Ruckman?" Because that is how Mohammed described his first encounter with the "Gabriel" who supposedly gave him the[ Koran.]{.class_1926} Unlike Daniel (or any other prophet in the Book, for that matter), Mohammed never received anything from God [personally;]{.class_1926} everything he got from "Allah" came through a 600-winged "angel" that called himself "Gabriel" ([Hadith,]{.class_1926} Bukhari, Vol. VI, no. 380). The first time "Gabriel" appeared to Mohammed, he [strangled]{.class_1926} Allah's "prophet" three times (A. Guillaume, [The Life of Mohammed,]{.class_1926} Oxford University Press, 2001, pg. 106). Whenever "Gabriel" would speak to Mohammed, the "prophet" would "hear ringing in his ears; his heart would beat rapidly; his face turned red; his breathing was labored; he would fall to the ground or lie down; he would shake; his eyes would open wide; his lips trembled; spit drooled from the corners of his mouth; he would sweat profusely; he saw and heard things no one else ever saw or heard; and he would sometimes make a snoring noise like that of a camel" ([Hadith,]{.class_1926} Bukhari, Vol. I, nos. 1--4; Vol. II no. 544; Vol. III, Nos. 17, 829; Vol. IV, nos. 95, 438, 458, 461; Vol. V, nos. 170, 462, 618, 659; Vol. VI, []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1200.xhtml_page_190}nos. 447--448, 468, 478, 481, 508). In other words, he acted like a crazed, demon-possessed epileptic; and I say that with apologies to every saved epileptic out there who loves the Lord and believes the Book, and who comes by his neurological disorder "honestly." Mohammed reacted like no prophet in that Book reacted, including the two men who actually saw the [real]{.class_1926} angel Gabriel.

19 And he said, Behold, I will make thee know what shall be in the last end of the indignation: for at the time appointed the end shall be.

20 The ram which thou sawest having two horns are the kings of Media and Persia.

21 And the rough goat is the king of Grecia: and the great horn that is between his eyes is the first king.

22 Now that being broken, whereas four stood up for it, four kingdoms shall stand up out of the nation, but not in his power.

23 And in the latter time of their kingdom, when the transgressors are come to the full, a king of fierce countenance, and understanding dark sentences, shall stand up.

24 And his power shall be mighty, but not by his own power: and he shall destroy wonderfully, and shall prosper, and practise, and shall destroy the mighty and the holy people.

25 And through his policy also he shall cause craft to prosper in his hand; and he shall magnify himself in his heart, and by peace shall destroy many: he shall also stand up against the Prince of princes; but he shall be broken without hand.

26 And the vision of the evening and the morning which was told is true: wherefore shut thou up the vision; for it shall be for many days.

Now I have chosen a larger portion here on which to comment because much of the material has already been covered back up in our exposition of Daniel's vision, and I refer you back to our []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1200.xhtml_page_191}comments on verses 3--12.

The word ["rough"]{.class_1922} in verse 21 can have one of two meanings. In English, [rough]{.class_1921} can mean "having an uneven or irregular surface." The Hebrew word here ([saiyr]{.class_1921}) can refer to the goat's coarse hairy coat. A better understanding, though, is the other meaning of [rough:]{.class_1921} "violent or boisterous." That certainly fits the disposition of the ["he goat"]{.class_1922} as given back up in verses 6--7.

Again, note the time period in view: ["in the latter time of their kingdom"]{.class_1922} (vs. 23). It goes far beyond the division of the Greek Empire right before Julius Caesar comes in. This is ["the times of the Gentiles"]{.class_1922} mentioned by Christ in Luke 21:24. Note the ["when the transgressors are come to the full"]{.class_1922} there in the same verse. That is what Paul calls ["the fulness of the Gentiles"]{.class_1922} right before the Second Advent (Rom. 11:25--26). So there is far more to the vision than Persia, Greece, Antiochus Epiphanes, or Rome.

Paul says, ["This know also, that in the last days perilous times shall come"]{.class_1922} (2 Tim. 3:1). You are living in those times. You have stuff on television now that would have taken an act of Congress to be broadcast when I was a kid. You have wicked stuff going on now [legally]{.class_1921} that would have sent the perpetrator to prison or an insane asylum when I was a boy. The sodomites, sex perverts, cross-dressers, and transvestites have taken over Western civilization, including the United States of America. Well, the Lord told you that conditions in the world before the Second Coming would be like those of Sodom before the fire fell (Luke 17:28--29). When the ["iniquity of the Amorites"]{.class_1922} became ["full,"]{.class_1922} God sent in the Israelites to wipe them out (Gen. 15:16). The Lord did the same thing to His own people when they lived that way (2 Kings 17:7--20). Do you think He's going to let this nation off? Don't bet your life on it (Psa. 9:17; Prov. 14:34). Do you know what you can expect from God Almighty for this nation? Unsheeted hell, brother!

["A king of fierce countenance."]{.class_1922} That's how the Holy Ghost described the Babylonians the Lord sent to judge His people (Deut. 28:50). When the Antichrist shows up, he is going to unleash such fury on the Jewish people that it will make Hitler's Holocaust look like a Sunday school picnic. There are a little over six million Jews in []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1200.xhtml_page_192}Israel right now. When the Devil's King gets through with them, I would venture to say there won't even be a thousand left when their Messiah comes back (Zech. 12:10--11). If you want to see what they can expect, read the book of Lamentations.

["Understanding dark sentences."]{.class_1922} The Hebrew word for ["dark sentences"]{.class_1922} ([chiydah]{.class_1921}) is the same word translated ["hard questions"]{.class_1922} in 1 Kings 10:1. In other words, he will seemingly be able to solve all the world's problems. Of course, it is Satanic power that gives him his wisdom (Rev. 13:4 cf. Ezek. 28:3--17), and God's commentary on this type of wisdom is found in 1 Corinthians 1:19--20, 3:19--20---READ IT!

We have already commented on the content of verse 24 in the two previous paragraphs. Once more, the cross-references are Revelation 13:2, 4; 2 Thessalonians 2:8--9; and Revelation 12:17, 13:7. The Antichrist gets his power from Satan for the purpose of committing [genocide]{.class_1921} on the Jews.

Did you ever stop to think about the Devil's singleness of purpose? You have to admire the Devil for his [tenacity.]{.class_1921} If you went after souls to win them to Christ as tenaciously as the Devil goes after them to destroy and damn them, you could really get something done for the Lord. One Christian said to another Christian one time, "You never criticize anybody; you are always looking for the good in everybody. Why, I think you would even speak well of the Devil." "Well, you have to admit, he is [persistent,"]{.class_1921} was the reply.

["And through his POLICY also he shall cause CRAFT to prosper in his hand"]{.class_1922} (vs. 25). This is the only use of the word ["policy"]{.class_1922} in your Bible ([AV]{.class_1921} 1611). It is defined as "a course or principle of action adopted or proposed by a [government."]{.class_1921} It is the current "buzzword" in [politics:]{.class_1921} "economic [policy,"]{.class_1921} "foreign [policy,"]{.class_1921} "social[ policy,"]{.class_1921} etc. Notice those words [policy]{.class_1921} and [politics,]{.class_1921} as [police]{.class_1921} and the suffix [polis]{.class_1921} on a word like metro[polis,]{.class_1921} all come from the Greek word [polis,]{.class_1921} meaning "city." Do you know who the first "city dweller" in the Bible was? It was [Cain,]{.class_1921} the first type of the Antichrist in that Book (1 John 3:12 cf. 2 Thess. 2:3, 8). This ["little horn"]{.class_1922} is a ruler of a one-world government under the [Devil,]{.class_1921} and he is connected with a [city]{.class_1921}---Babylon (Rev. 17--18).

This verse is also the first mention of the word ["craft"]{.class_1922} in the []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1200.xhtml_page_193}Scriptures. The word means "an activity involving skill in making things by hand," and that is how the word is used in Acts 18:3. At one time, workers used to pride themselves on the "craftsmanship" of the things they made; like musical instruments, furniture, pottery, etc. But with the need to drive down costs through inferior materials and cheaper labor, in order to compete with products imported from places like Japan, Korea, and China, craftsmanship gradually fell to the wayside. There are still products out there that demonstrate a high level of craftsmanship (like jewelry), but you will pay a high price for them.

Now between the war and famine that will show up during the Tribulation (see Rev. 6:4--6), you can expect a worldwide economic collapse that will make the Great Depression of the 1930s look like a walk in the park. This certainly would explain why the False Prophet restricts the buying and selling to those who receive the mark in Revelation 13:16--17. You starve out any rebellion or "fifth column."

The Antichrist will restore the world's economy not through Wall Street in New York or London or Tokyo or the World Bank, but through [Babylon]{.class_1921} (Rev. 18:3). That is why Larkin distinguishes between a religious Babylon in Revelation 17 and an economic Babylon in Revelation 18. That may or may not be so, but what is so is that the last time the words ["craftsman"]{.class_1922} and ["craft"]{.class_1922} appear in your Bible is in Revelation 18:22 in connection with [Babylon.]{.class_1921}

But there is much more to this word ["craft"]{.class_1922} in Daniel 8:25 than just "handcrafted" furniture or "handcrafted" clocks or "handcrafted" jewelry. Look at the first time the companion word [craftsman]{.class_1921} appears in your Bible.

["Cursed be the man that MAKETH ANY GRAVEN OR MOLTEN IMAGE, an abomination unto the LORD, THE WORKS OF THE HANDS OF THE CRAFTSMAN, and putteth it in a secret place. And all the people shall answer and say, Amen"]{.class_1922} (Deut. 27:25).

There, the "craft" was [constructing idols.]{.class_1921} You will see the same thing in Hosea 13:2 and Acts 19:24, 38. By the way, those ["craftsmen"]{.class_1922} there in Acts 19 who made ["silver shrines for Diana"]{.class_1922} (Acts 19:24) worshiped ["the image which fell down from Jupiter"]{.class_1922} (Acts 19:35). So when Satan comes down from outer []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1200.xhtml_page_194}space with his angels (Rev. 12:4, 9, 12 cf. Gen. 6:2--4), he has his False Prophet build an image of his son (Rev. 13:14--15 cf. 2 Thess. 2:3--9). The ["policy"]{.class_1922} that causes the ["craft to prosper"]{.class_1922} is worship the Antichrist and his image or get your head chopped off (Rev. 13:15, cf. Rev. 20:4). Not only will there be the chief image set up by the False Prophet, there will be a whole slew of little images made by craftsmen. If you can't make it to worship the big one, at least you can worship one of the little ones. And if you don't, off goes your head.

Now think about that for a moment. The world has been broken by war, by famine, and by Hell on earth (Rev. 6). People are dying right and left from what will be labeled by Christ-rejecting news reporters as "natural disasters" (Rev. 8). In the middle of all that destruction and chaos, the "answer" to all the world's problems will be to worship a totalitarian dictator upon pain of death. The whole economy will be based on it. Crops, livestock, natural resources, industry, and national security will take a backseat to [that.]{.class_1921}

So when the Lord Jesus Christ returns, one of the first things He does is get rid of all the idols (see our comments on Hab. 2:18--20 in that Commentary). When those ["kings," "great men," "rich men," "chief captains," "mighty men," ]{.class_1922}slaves, and free men are trying to hide in caves and under rocks ["from the wrath of the Lamb"]{.class_1922} (Rev. 6:15--16), do you know what they are trying to do? They are trying to get rid of their idols just as quickly as they can; they don't want to be caught "red-handed" with them. Out go the "Madonnas," the "pietas," the "crucifixes," and the "saints" (along with Buddha, Kali, Shiva, the Black Stone in the Kaaba, "icons," "oscars," "grammies," "emmies," and "American Idol") ["to the moles and to the bats"]{.class_1922} (Isa. 2:19--20). The idols will be cut off and not even their names will be remembered (Zech. 13:2).

Back to Daniel 8:25---["And he shall magnify himself in his heart]{.class_1922} \[see our comments on vs. 11\][, and BY PEACE SHALL DESTROY MANY."]{.class_1922} That's the mark of the Devil---all [positive.]{.class_1921} The first word the Devil speaks when he shows up in Scripture the first time is [yes ]{.class_1921}(["Yea"]{.class_1922}---Gen. 3:1). When the Antichrist shows up, he conquers through "peace" (Dan. 11:21)---he is a bowman with [no arrows]{.class_1921} (Rev. 6:2). The hand symbol for peace is two fingers up. That's no "peace" sign. It's the signal for an [assault]{.class_1921}[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1200.xhtml_page_195} in the military (such as a bayonet assault or a tank assault). It is the sign of a [Syrian]{.class_1921} bowman, who pulled his bowstring back with the first two fingers. That is your "papal blessing." It's not a sign of "peace"; it's a sign that all hell's about to break loose.

This Man of Sin shows up praying for world peace and "make me an instrument of Thy peace" and saying, "Peace to men of good will." But though he says, ["Peace, peace,"]{.class_1922} ["there is NO PEACE"]{.class_1922} (Jer. 6:14, 8:11). ["There is no peace, saith my God, to the wicked"]{.class_1922} (Isa. 57:21, 48:22). So when someone like this ["little horn"]{.class_1922} speaks ["peace,"]{.class_1922} it is actually for the purpose of ["mischief"]{.class_1922} (Psa. 28:3) and ["war"]{.class_1922} (Psa. 55:21).

The Apostle Paul wrote, ["For when they shall say, Peace and safety, then sudden destruction cometh upon them, as travail upon a woman with child; and they shall not escape"]{.class_1922} (1 Thess. 5:3).

This ["little horn"]{.class_1922} is a counterfeit "Prince of peace," which is why he stands up against the [real]{.class_1921}[ "Prince of Peace"]{.class_1922} here in verse 25 of Daniel 8. ["But he shall be broken without hand."]{.class_1922} That's [literal.]{.class_1921} The sword with which Jesus Christ smites this ["little horn"]{.class_1922} comes ["out of his mouth,"]{.class_1922} not His hands (Rev. 19:15).[ "The God of peace"]{.class_1922} bruises Satan incarnate under His [feet,]{.class_1921} not His hands (Rom. 16:20; Gen. 3:15; Rev. 14:20; Isa. 63:3; Zech. 14:4).

Verse 26:[ "And the vision of the evening and the morning which was told is true."]{.class_1922} Now back under my remarks on verse 14, I told you those ["days"]{.class_1922} weren't "prophetic days," but literal 24-hour days. If you had been reading any other commentary that took that position, the expositor would have taken you to the Hebrew word for ["days"]{.class_1922} in that verse ([ereb]{.class_1921}) and would have shown you the word means "morning and evening." That is not necessarily wrong or an incorrect use of "the Hebrew" at that point, but you didn't need to know Hebrew to interpret the verse correctly. Verse 26 defines the words ["daily"]{.class_1922} and ["days"]{.class_1922} for you in the vision: ["the evening and the morning"]{.class_1922}---a Hebrew day just like you read it in Genesis 1.

["The vision . . . is true"]{.class_1922} because it is part of ["the scripture of truth"]{.class_1922} (10:21) and ["the word of truth"]{.class_1922} (Psa. 119:43; 2 Cor. 6:7; Eph. 1:13; 2 Tim. 2:15; James 1:18). ["Sanctify them through thy truth: thy word is truth"]{.class_1922} (John 17:17). []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1200.xhtml_page_196}["All thy commandments are truth"]{.class_1922} (Psa. 119:151); ["thy law is the truth"]{.class_1922} (Psa. 119:142). ["Thy word is true from the beginning"]{.class_1922} (Psa. 119:160).

["Wherefore shut thou up the vision; for it shall be for many days."]{.class_1922} This is what Daniel was told about the words of the book in Daniel 12:4, and they weren't to be opened until ["the time of the end."]{.class_1922} So this vision here in Daniel 8 goes far beyond the intertestamental period. I get that by comparing Scripture with Scripture (1 Cor. 2:13).

27 And I Daniel fainted, and was sick certain days; afterward I rose up, and did the king's business; and I was astonished at the vision, but none understood it.

Daniel was so troubled over the vision that he fainted and became sick (see our comments on 7:28). When Daniel tells others what he had seen, there was nobody, [including Daniel,]{.class_1921} who ["understood it"]{.class_1922} (vs. 27). That's because the vision was shut up until ["the time of the end"]{.class_1922} (12:4, 9 cf. Rev. 22:10). So even though Gabriel had explained the vision to Daniel (vss. 16--17), there were things even in the explanation on which the Holy Spirit had not given light.

Brethren, the Holy Spirit hasn't revealed everything in that Book to any one man, [including me.]{.class_1921} The pastor of the Pilgrims, John Robinson, said, ["The Lut]{.class_1934}[herans . . . could not go beyond what Luther saw . . . So,]{.class_1927} also, you see the Calvinists, they stick where he \[i.e., John Calvin\] left them . . . they \[Calvin and Luther\] were precious shining lights in their times, yet God did not reveal His whole will to them . . . ." He went on to say that God "hath more truth and light yet to breake forth out of his holy Word." Don't get bogged down with Larkin, Scofield, Bullinger, Torrey, Pember, Pentecost, LaHaye, Lindsey, Kirban, or [Ruckman.]{.class_1921} Get into the word yourself and let the Holy Spirit show you for yourself what's in there.

[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1271.xhtml}

# Chapter 9 {.heading_67-0}

9:1 In the first year of Darius the son of Ahasuerus, of the seed of the Medes, which was made king over the realm of the Chaldeans;

2 In the first year of his reign I Daniel understood by books the number of the years, whereof the word of the LORD came to Jeremiah the prophet, that he would accomplish seventy years in the desolations of Jerusalem.

We are now, chronologically, back in Daniel 6 (["In the first year of Darius," ]{.class_1922}vs. 1). Verse 1 is the only place in Daniel where the father of Darius the Mede is given, but it is not a proper name. ["Ahasuerus"]{.class_1922} was a [title]{.class_1921} (meaning "Prince," "head," "chief") given to three Kings in the Bible: the father of Darius the Mede here, the King in Ezra 4:6, and the King of the book of Esther. Most scholars identify the ["Ahasuerus"]{.class_1922} of verse 1 as a Median General named Astyages (spelled Asteiages by Bullinger), who had conquered Nineveh.

There is nothing necessarily wrong with that view, but Bullinger makes the Ahasuerus of Daniel 9:1 the same as the Ahasuerus of Esther. In fact, Bullinger has the whole book of Esther take place between Daniel chapters 4 and 5, and he has Esther as the mother of Cyrus the Persian. That is not true [historically,]{.class_1921} and it is not true [Scripturally.]{.class_1921} Astyages was a [Mede]{.class_1921} who ruled from a [Median]{.class_1921} city (Ecbatana), not the [Persian]{.class_1921} capital of Shushan (see our comments on 8:2). His [Median]{.class_1921} daughter (Mandane of Media), not Esther the [Jewess,]{.class_1921} was the mother of Cyrus, and she wasn't married to Astyages ([Cambyses I]{.class_1921} was the father of Cyrus).

Astyages ruled over [Media,]{.class_1921} not ["from India even unto Ethiopia"]{.class_1922} (Esth. 1:1), and his kingdom didn't have 127 provinces (Esth. 1:1). Those were set up by Darius (see our comments on 6:1). Moreover, Media didn't have control over the Jewish captivity in Daniel 4--5; Babylon did. Bullinger is just as fouled up as a Chinese fire drill.

Verse 2: ["I Daniel understood by books."]{.class_1922} The ["books,"]{.class_1922} here, turn out to be the prophecy of Jeremiah. These []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1271.xhtml_page_198}["books"]{.class_1922} would be scrolls containing the various parts of the book of Jeremiah (cf. Jer. 36:2, 4, 6, 32). Daniel gained understanding by [reading the Scriptures.]{.class_1921} David wrote, ["give me understanding ACCORDING TO THY WORD"]{.class_1922} (Psa. 119:169). There is nothing necessarily wrong with reading commentaries and the works of Bible teachers, but there is nothing like a Bible to clear up a commentary or a Seminary education.

Now look at that. Jeremiah finally got himself a convert. Jeremiah only had two converts about whom he knew anything: Baruch and a black fellow named Ebedmelech. But Jeremiah had some converts of whom he wasn't even aware: Daniel, Shadrach, Meshach, and Abednego. Where did they get the courage not to compromise? They got it from Jeremiah! While Jehoiakim was cutting up the Scriptures and living like hell (Jer. 36), Jeremiah was making an impression on some boys there in the King's court. Of course, they might not have taken heed to it at the time (see our comments on vs. 5), but when they got hauled off to Babylon, they recalled the old preacher and determined they would follow his example.

I have a sermon entitled "Not Now, But Afterwards." In other words, you might not see the results of your preaching or ministry right away, but the results will pop up sometime down the road. You just keep "casting your bread on the waters," and ["thou shalt find it after many days"]{.class_1922} (Eccl. 11:1). Jeremiah was still reaping a harvest nearly seventy years after his ministry was over.

The Scriptures Daniel is reading are Jeremiah 25:11--12 and 29:10. God sent those Jews into captivity for seventy years because the entire time they had had a King (1096 B.C.---when Saul began his reign), they had never observed the year of rest every seventh year commanded in the Law (Lev. 25:2--4). The Lord promised the captivity would last a year for every sabbatical year neglected (Lev. 26:34--35, 43), and that's exactly what happened (2 Chron. 36:21). It was 490 years from the beginning of Saul's reign (1096 B.C.) to when the captivity began in Daniel 1:1 (606 B.C.); that's ["seventy times seven"]{.class_1922} (see our comments on Matt. 18:22 in that Commentary). The reason that is so significant is because you are about to run into []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1271.xhtml_page_199}the same thing again down in verses 24--27 here in Daniel 9, and it will date [both Advents of Christ.]{.class_1921}

3 And I set my face unto the Lord God, to seek by prayer and supplications, with fasting, and sackcloth, and ashes:

4 And I prayed unto the LORD my God, and made my confession, and said, O Lord, the great and dreadful God, keeping the covenant and mercy to them that love him, and to them that keep his commandments;

5 We have sinned, and have committed iniquity, and have done wickedly, and have rebelled, even by departing from thy precepts and from thy judgments:

6 Neither have we hearkened unto thy servants the prophets, which spake in thy name to our kings, our princes, and our fathers, and to all the people of the land.

Verse 3 introduces one of the great penitential prayers in the Bible. Daniel's prayer, here, takes its place alongside Ezra's prayer in Ezra 9, Nehemiah's prayer in Nehemiah 1, and David's prayer in Psalm 51. It is unlike any prayer offered at the "National Day of Prayer." Look at verses 5--6.

1. ["We have sinned"]{.class_1922} (vs. 5).

2. ["Have committed iniquity"]{.class_1922} (vs. 5).

3. ["Have done wickedly"]{.class_1922} (vs. 5).

4. ["Have rebelled"]{.class_1922} (vs. 5).

5. ["By departing from thy precepts and from thy judgments"]{.class_1922} (vs. 5).

6. ["Neither have we hearkened unto thy servants the prophets"]{.class_1922} (vs. 6).

That's six confessions of sin in the first sentence of the prayer. The official prayer of the 2016 National Day of Prayer has repentance in it twice, but never says what anybody is repenting of. There is no mention of sin or iniquity or wickedness or rebellion against the written and spoken words of God at all; just "carnality." That's because a "committee" is trying to unite a coalition of Liberals, New Evangelicals, Neo-orthodox, Charismatics, Fundamentalists, Conservatives, Reformed, and Catholics around []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1271.xhtml_page_200}"prayer." If mention were made against the sins of those groups (especially in forsaking the God-honored English Bible of the Reformation), it would bust the whole thing up. So all you have are vague generalities that can mean anything to anyone. Daniel is not worried about any ecumenical union. All he's worried about are Leviticus 26:40--42; Deuteronomy 30:1--3; and 2 Chronicles 6:37--38.

It is a [long]{.class_1921} prayer: it goes from verse 4 to verse 19. It is a [serious]{.class_1921} prayer: Daniel fasts and puts on ["sackcloth, and ashes"]{.class_1922} to show he means business (vs. 3). It is a [personal]{.class_1921} prayer:[ ]{.class_1935}["MY God," "MY confession" ]{.class_1922}(vs. 4). It's not just about other people; like the old Negro spiritual says, "It's me, it's me, it's me, O Lord, standing in the need of prayer."

Notice in verse 4 that Jehovah (["LORD"]{.class_1922}) is the ["Lord."]{.class_1922} The reason that is so significant is because the Jehovah's Witnesses try to make a distinction between Jehovah (LORD) and Adonai (Lord) that is not found in the Bible---Hebrew or English. The classic case to which they will take you is Psalm 110:1, where Jehovah and Adonai are two separate people. Of course, the Bible believer recognizes this as a reference to the [Trinity]{.class_1921} (Father and Son). Adonai is [not]{.class_1921} a separate Lord or God from Jehovah, though, as is evidenced here in Daniel 9:4. See also Genesis 18:26--27, 32--33; Exodus 4:10, 5:22; Joshua 3:13; Nehemiah 10:29; and Psalm 8:1, 9. And of course, Jesus Christ is the Jehovah God of the Old Testament (Isa. 44:6 cf. Rev. 1:11, 17, 2:8, 22:13; John 17:3 cf. 1 John 5:20; Zech. 12:4--10 cf. Rev. 1:7).

Notice also that Daniel doesn't approach the Lord with the flippant attitude of modern Christianity. The Lord God is not anybody's "Buddy" in the sky (or as one Christian wit put it: "Jesus is not your bearded girlfriend"). He's ["the great and dreadful God"]{.class_1922} (vs. 4). You approach Him not only ["with reverence,"]{.class_1922} but with ["godly fear"]{.class_1922} (Heb. 12:28), showing you that the fear of the Lord (commanded in the New Testament for the believer in Christ---2 Cor. 7:1; Eph. 5:21; 1 Pet. 2:17) is [something different]{.class_1921} than reverencing God. This modern bunch of Laodiceans forget that the crucifixion of Christ is not only a display of God's love for the sinner, it's also a display of [His wrath toward sin.]{.class_1921} A man is a fool not to fear a Being []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1271.xhtml_page_201}who thinks so harshly of sin that He would submit His own Son to go through what He went through on the cross to pay for that sin.

["Keeping the covenant and mercy to them that love him, and to them that keep his commandments."]{.class_1922} This is a  reference to the covenant made with Israel when they came out of Egypt (Jer. 31:32). It was made with them at Sinai when God gave them the Ten Commandments (Deut. 5:2--21). Unlike the Abrahamic covenant which was [unconditional]{.class_1921} (see our comments on Gen. 15:12--18 and Psa. 105:8--11 in their respective Commentaries), the Mosaic covenant was [conditional.]{.class_1921} It was, if Israel would forsake all other gods and worship only Jehovah and keep His commandments, God would show mercy on them and give them the land promised to Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob, and bless them in it (Exod. 19:5--6, 20:3--6; Lev. 26:1--9; Deut. 7:9--16). And if they didn't, He would curse them and turn them over to their enemies to be taken out of the Promised Land (Lev. 26:14--33; Deut. 4:25--28, 28:58--64; 2 Kings 17:7--23). The promise was, though, that if they repented and confessed their sins in the land of their captivity, God would hear them and restore them. This was particularly true of the Babylonian Captivity (Jer. 29:12--14), but there is also a prophetic application that still awaits fulfillment at the Second Advent.

["But if from thence ]{.class_1922}\[their captivity---Deut. 4:27\][ thou shalt seek the LORD thy God, thou shalt find him, if thou seek him with all thy heart and with all thy soul. When thou art IN TRIBULATION, and all these things are come upon thee, EVEN IN THE LATTER DAYS, if thou turn to the LORD thy God, and shalt be obedient unto his voice; (For the LORD thy God is a merciful God;) he will not forsake thee, neither destroy thee, nor forget the covenant of thy fathers which he sware unto them"]{.class_1922} (Deut. 4:29--31).

As we will see, this penitential prayer of Daniel leads into a prophecy about the Second Advent. So the first restoration of Israel to the land is a prophetic type of a second and final restoration of the Jews to their homeland (Isa. 11:11). And just as the first restoration eventually culminated in the First Advent of Jesus Christ, the second restoration will eventually culminate in the Second Advent of Jesus Christ. That is where you are now.

["WE have sinned"]{.class_1922} (vs. 5). It is a prayer of [national]{.class_1921}[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1271.xhtml_page_202} repentance---see the references to ["Judah," "Jerusalem,"]{.class_1922} and ["Israel"]{.class_1922} in verse 7. But at the same time, the implication is that Daniel himself had a part in the sin, rebellion, and disregard for God's prophets (cf. Neh. 1:6). Daniel is reading Jeremiah's prophecy, but he implies, in verse 6, that while he was still a boy back in Jerusalem, he himself did not take heed to Jeremiah's preaching. So becoming eunuchs in the court of Nebuchadnezzar was a "wake-up call" to Daniel and his three buddies. Blessed is the man who recognizes the chastening hand of the Lord and responds correctly to it (Heb. 12:5--13), and blessed is the young man who learns that lesson at an early age. The best thing is to get saved when you are around five years old; if you are going to backslide, do it when you are around ten; then get right before you're twelve and stay right.

7 O Lord, righteousness belongeth unto thee, but unto us confusion of faces, as at this day; to the men of Judah, and to the inhabitants of Jerusalem, and unto all Israel, that are near, and that are far off, through all the countries whither thou hast driven them, because of their trespass that they have trespassed against thee.

8 O Lord, to us belongeth confusion of face, to our kings, to our princes, and to our fathers, because we have sinned against thee.

9 To the Lord our God belong mercies and forgivenesses, though we have rebelled against him;

Verse 7 is the key to understanding Acts 2:38--39 and getting it [right.]{.class_1921} The Campbellite will take you to Acts 2:38 as the plan of salvation for this age, and his justification for that will be ["all that are afar off"]{.class_1922} in Acts 2:39. Before we go splashing around, though, in the Water Dog bathtub, let's get the Holy Spirit's take on ["all that are afar off,"]{.class_1922} instead of the private interpretation of some "elder" trying to appropriate the blood of Christ through the city water system.

First, there are no "Christians" in Acts 2---before or after verse 38; no "Christian" shows up in the entire Bible until you get to Acts 11:26. Peter is preaching to [Jews]{.class_1921} at [Jerusalem]{.class_1921}[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1271.xhtml_page_203} (Acts 2:5, 14), who are members of the nation of [Israel]{.class_1921} (Acts 2:22). Now go back and look at to whom Daniel 9:7 is addressed: ["to the men of JUDAH]{.class_1922} \[there's your Judean Jews\][, and to the inhabitants of JERUSALEM]{.class_1922} \[there are those Jerusalem dwellers\][, and unto ALL ISRAEL]{.class_1922} \[and there are Peter's ["men of Israel"]{.class_1922}\][, and that are FAR OFF]{.class_1922} \[Gentiles? Don't be waterlogged, with water on the brain, like a Campbellite Water Dog\][, through all the countries whither thou hast driven THEM]{.class_1922} \[Jews ["out of every nation"]{.class_1922} in Acts 2:5\]["]{.class_1922}---Jews of the [Dispersion,]{.class_1921} just like in Acts 2:39.

The Campbellite will run over to Ephesians 2 and read verses 16--17 back into Acts 2:38--39, even though Paul had not written anything yet and no ["gospel of the grace of God"]{.class_1931} had been preached to any Gentile yet (see Acts 20:24). The only Gentiles in Acts 2 were [proselytes to Judaism]{.class_1932} (Acts 2:10). The same apostle who wrote Ephesians 2:16--17 told you that ["the promise of the Spirit"]{.class_1931} comes ["on the Gentiles" "THROUGH FAITH,"]{.class_1931} [not water baptism]{.class_1932} (Gal. 3:14). Peter doesn't have anything Paul ever wrote in mind in Acts 2. Paul wasn't even saved yet and hadn't had anything revealed to him yet. Peter is operating from the only revelation he has, and that revelation matches [Daniel 9:7.]{.class_1932}

Verses 7--8 contrast God's righteousness with the trespasses and sins of the Jews from the leaders all the way to the Jews dispersed among the Gentile nations. The idea is that God was just and right in His judgments against His people, and this is brought out in Leviticus 26:40--42; Nehemiah 9:33; and Lamentations 1:18. The spiritual application in the New Testament is to admit that you are a sinner under the just condemnation of God and that you cannot save yourself by your own righteousness; you have to receive the righteousness of God through His Son (Rom. 3:20--26, 10:3--10; Tit. 3:5).

Notice the "power of negative thinking" in the passage. It's the righteousness of God and the condemnation of the sinner [first]{.class_1921} (vss. 7--8), and [then]{.class_1921} it's mercy and forgiveness (vs. 9). If you won't come to God as a sinner in need of a Saviour, you will stay in bondage with no mercy, no forgiveness, and [no hope]{.class_1921} (Eph. 2:12). Those of us who have experienced the richness of God's mercy (Eph. 2:4), realized first that we were []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1271.xhtml_page_204}["dead in trespasses and sins," "children of disobedience"]{.class_1922} under the wrath of God (Eph. 2:1--3). That's when we could come to Christ for a spiritual resurrection that put us in Him, where He is (Eph. 2:5--6), by grace through faith in what He did for us and not by our own works (Eph. 2:8--9).

That's what happened to me on March 14, 1949. The Lord had been working me over for a month from a stolen Bible when Hugh Pyle witnessed to me in the record room of WEAR. When Bro. Pyle asked me if I knew I was a sinner, there was no doubt in my mind I was a sinner. In fact, all I was able to find in that Book in the four weeks previous to that was condemnation for my sin. So yeah, I[ knew]{.class_1921} I was a sinner. When that preacher asked me to take his hand and pray in my own words for Jesus Christ to save me, I said, "God, I know I am a blankety-blank sinner, and I want you to save me; and if you don't save me pretty blankety-blank quick, I'm going to Hell just as sure as blankety-blank."

I cussed all the way through the prayer, but I meant what I said. Hugh Pyle had a lot of wisdom, and instead of chiding me for my foul mouth (which was second nature to me by then), he took me to 1 John 5:13 and grounded my faith [in what God said,]{.class_1921} not what I said. After all, I wasn't trusting my prayer to save me; I was trusting [Jesus Christ,]{.class_1921}[ "the righteousness of God"]{.class_1922} (2 Cor. 5:21).

10 Neither have we obeyed the voice of the LORD our God, to walk in his laws, which he set before us by his servants the prophets.

11 Yea, all Israel have transgressed thy law, even by departing, that they might not obey thy voice; therefore the curse is poured upon us, and the oath that is written in the law of Moses the servant of God, because we have sinned against him.

12 And he hath confirmed his words, which he spake against us, and against our judges that judged us, by bringing upon us a great evil: for under the whole heaven hath not been done as hath been done upon Jerusalem.

13 As it is written in the law of Moses, all this evil is come upon us: yet made we not our prayer before the []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1271.xhtml_page_205}LORD our God, that we might turn from our iniquities, and understand thy truth.

14 Therefore hath the LORD watched upon the evil, and brought it upon us: for the LORD our God is righteous in all his works which he doeth: for we obeyed not his voice.

15 And now, O Lord our God, that hast brought thy people forth out of the land of Egypt with a mighty hand, and hast gotten thee renown, as at this day; we have sinned, we have done wickedly.

You have not heard anyone in America in the past sixty years confess sins like that. None of the TV preachers do it, including the few good ones on the air. When was the last time you heard anyone get up and say, "Lord, every one of us here in America has disobeyed you, rebelled against you, broken your laws, rejected your Bible, and ignored your preachers"? Well, that's what you would need to say if you misappropriated 2 Chronicles 7:14 for professing Christians under a Socialistic oligarchy (formerly a democratic, constitutional republic) instead of a Jewish theocracy set up by God Almighty.

Probably the closest you have come was a prayer offered up by a Kansas pastor named Joe Wright. Back in January of 1996, he was asked to open the Kansas House of Representatives in prayer, and this was his prayer:

"Heavenly Father, we come before You today to ask Your forgiveness and seek Your direction and guidance. Lord, we know your Word says, 'Woe to those who call evil good,' but that's exactly what we've done. We have lost our spiritual equilibrium and inverted our values.

"We confess that we have ridiculed the absolute truth of Your Word and called it moral pluralism.

"We have worshiped other gods and called it multiculturalism.

"We have endorsed perversion and called it an alternative lifestyle.

"We have exploited the poor and called it the lottery.

"We have neglected the needy and called it self-preservation.

"We have rewarded laziness and called it welfare.

"We have killed our unborn and called it choice.

"We have shot abortionists and called it justifiable.

"We have neglected to discipline our children and called it building esteem.

"We have abused power and called it political savvy.

"We have coveted our neighbors' possessions and called it ambition.

"We have polluted the air with profanity and pornography and called it freedom of expression.

"We have ridiculed the time-honored values of our forefathers and called it enlightenment.

"Search us, oh God, and know our hearts today; try us and see if there be some wicked way in us; cleanse us from every sin and set us free.

"Guide and bless these men and women who have been sent here by the people of Kansas, and who have been ordained by You, to govern this great state. Grant them Your wisdom to rule and may their decisions direct us to the center of Your will. I ask it in the name of Your Son, the Living Saviour, Jesus Christ. Amen."

For the day and age in which we live, that's a pretty good prayer. It certainly offended a bunch of Democratic thin-skinned sissies. One Democrat walked out on the prayer, and four others got up afterwards and criticized it for its "intolerance" and "partisanship." They would have gone absolutely "ballistic" had Daniel been praying. Wright's prayer was tame compared to Daniel's here in chapter 9. Wright [insinuated]{.class_1921} they all had sinned, but he never outright said it. He said they called evil good; he asked God to see IF there were some wicked way in them; he asked for cleansing from every sin; but he never actually said, "We have sinned." Daniel said it in every way he could think of: "We've sinned; we've committed iniquity; we've transgressed; we've rebelled; we've departed from you; we haven't listened to you; we've disobeyed; we've trespassed; we've done wickedly."

There was no doubt, when Daniel got through praying, that every Jew from Exodus on to the Babylonian Captivity was a dirty, low-down, filthy, rotten, stinking SINNER. ["Yea, ALL Israel have transgressed thy law"]{.class_1922} (vs. 11). No one was exempt. What we need today is someone to stand up and "read the riot act" to []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1271.xhtml_page_207}[everybody:]{.class_1921} the President, the Congressmen, the Senators, the "Secretaries" in the Cabinet, the candidates, the police, the Mayor, the soldiers, the sailors, the Marines, the airmen, the city council, the doctors, the lawyers, the bankers, the welfare recipients, the whites, the blacks, the Asians, the "native Americans," the immigrants, the citizens, the day laborers, the day traders, Wall Street, the "Bowery," skid row, the queers, the cross-genders, the Lesbians, the rapists, the murderers, the thieves, the teachers, the [preachers]{.class_1921} (let's not forget them!), the Pope, the Bishops, the Rabbis, the Imams---ALL OF THEM, brother! Note ["the voice of the LORD"]{.class_1922} in verse 10, and another reference to it in verse 11 (["thy voice"]{.class_1922}). It is a reference to the ["words"]{.class_1922} of God (vs. 12), not just His "Word" or "word." As I have pointed out to you on many an occasion, it is not just the Neo-orthodox "message" of the Bible or even the "word of God" as a whole. It is those W-O-R-D-S, [plural,]{.class_1921} that are pure and preserved (Psa. 12:6--7; Prov. 30:5), and that are spirit and life (John 6:63). The ["word"]{.class_1922} that God has magnified above His own name (Psa. 138:2) is made up of ["words"]{.class_1922} (Psa. 138:4), and it is Satan's goal to corrupt those words (2 Cor. 2:17) and steal them from you (Luke 8:11--12). He is aided these days by [Christian scholarship]{.class_1921}---Fundamental and Conservative foremost (see the [NASV]{.class_1921} and the [ESV]{.class_1921}).

Here, it is a reference to two things: the [written]{.class_1921} word of God in the Scriptures (vss. 11, 13) and the word of God as [spoken]{.class_1921} by the prophets. Of course, to us this side of the close of the canon of Scripture, it is all the written words of God in the Bible. The words that the ["holy men of God SPAKE as they were moved by the Holy Ghost"]{.class_1922} (2 Pet. 1:21) are recorded for us in the ["prophecy of the SCRIPTURE"]{.class_1922} (2 Pet. 1:20), and ["ALL SCRIPTURE]{.class_1922}[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1271.xhtml_page_208} \[not just "the originals" as the Christian scholars would have you believe\][ is given by inspiration of God, and is profitable"]{.class_1922} (2 Tim. 3:16). Do you have that ["scripture"]{.class_1922}? If only the "originals" were "inspired," then you don't. Timothy had them (2 Tim. 3:15), and he sure didn't have anything "original" Moses, Daniel, or Isaiah wrote.

Some of you poor saps out there teaching in Christian Colleges and Universities only have "reliable translations"; some might even profess to have "thoroughly reliable translations" which they have checked "word for word with the originals" (a lie; nobody living in the past 1900 years has seen anything "original" Paul wrote. What they mean is that they have checked it out with Nestle's or some other Greek text). Of course, their "thoroughly reliable" translation differs from the [Authorized Version]{.class_1921} (which is only "reliable") in about 36,000 ([NASV]{.class_1921}) to 64,000 ([NIV]{.class_1921}) places, but hey, who cares about every word of God anyway (Matt. 4:4)?

I, on the other hand, profess to have the very words God wants me to have in English. If you don't, [I do,]{.class_1921} and they are found in a [King James]{.class_1921} Bible from 1611---the Holy Scriptures in English. I am subject to those words, and not they to me. In other words, I actually believe what they profess and don't. They aren't subject to any book in print. They will change any word, in any Bible, they don't like or can't understand. That's why you have had 323-plus versions put out since 1880, and they will continue non-stop until the Devil incarnate shows up to run the UN and the Catholic Church.

["The curse . . . and oath that is written in the law of Moses"]{.class_1922} can be found in Leviticus 26:14--39 and Deuteronomy 27:15--26, 28:15--68, 29:20--28, 30:17--19, 32:19--26. One of the most horrible declarations in the whole Bible is Deuteronomy 28:63---["And it shall come to pass, that as the LORD rejoiced over you to do you good, and to multiply you; so the LORD will rejoice over you to destroy you, and bring you to nought."]{.class_1922} That's the Lord rejoicing over the destruction of His chosen people. Why? ["Because thou wouldest not obey the voice of the LORD thy God"]{.class_1922} (Deut. 28:62).

That's why you can't consign something like the Holocaust just to the machinations of a mad man like Hitler. Those Jews had the []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1271.xhtml_page_209}promise from God that if they were following what He said in His word, the Lord would protect them and give them victory over their enemies, and if they didn't, He Himself would turn them over to those who hated them.

If God would do that to His own chosen people, what do you think He's going to do with this country for going against that Book? Is there any soul so bold that he would say what Daniel did? "Our Supreme Court justices have sinned against you; our district court judges have sinned against you; our probate judges have sinned against you. Because of that, Lord, you've brought hurricanes, forest fires, tornadoes, school shootings, drought, and terrorists on this country; and you were right for doing it, Lord." Why, people like James Dobson, Rick Warren, Billy Graham, Joel Osteen, et al., wouldn't dare say anything like that; it would be bad for business (\$\$\$).

But that's what Daniel did: ["Therefore hath the LORD watched upon the evil ]{.class_1922}\[He tended it like a man would a fire he has set\][, and brought it upon us: for the LORD our God is righteous in all his works which he doeth"]{.class_1922} (vs. 14). Nebuchadnezzar came in and starved out Jerusalem, causing the women to eat their children in the siege. He burned down the Temple and left the city in rubble. He took the King (Zedekiah) captive, killed all of his sons in front of him, then put out his eyes and hauled him off to Babylon, where he died too. He hung up the old men by their thumbs; he let his men rape the women; he had the babies' brains bashed out against the rocks.

You say, "Who was responsible for all that?" God Almighty! He looked over it and made sure every bit of it happened. You say, "A loving God wouldn't let that sort of thing go on." But a [holy, righteous]{.class_1921} God sure would. He would drown out over 300 million people, including little children and "senior citizens," without blinking (Gen. 7). Why? ["For we obeyed not his voice."]{.class_1922}

Do you know why God was so harsh on His own people, and why this country will get the same treatment from Him? Because they had greater privileges from the Lord than any other nation on earth. They were descendants from Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob, to whom God promised the land. Their nation began like no other nation []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1271.xhtml_page_210}began---with the Book (Exod. 24:7--8). God chose Jerusalem to put His name and presence there. They had the Temple and the sacrifices. They had the Levites to teach them the Book. God sent them prophets. They had the blessings of God on their nation. They had to step over all those things to enter into God's judgment.

This nation is like that. Your Pilgrim forefathers came over here to be able to worship God according to that Book and not according to the whims of some man; whether in Rome, London, or Canterbury. They came over here with the Book and with the intent of taking the Book to the lost world. The founders of this nation may not have all been saved, but they recognized the authority of that Book and set up a government based on it. This nation has had more Bible, more Gospel, and more truth than any other nation on earth. As long as its people stood for the Book, God showered it with material, economic, and military prosperity. So now that this nation has dumped the Book, what do you think is going to happen? Well, I guarantee you it won't be "God Bless America." God will bring a curse on this country just like He brought a curse on His own people. The difference between the United States and Israel, though, is that the United States has [no promise of restoration as a nation as Israel does]{.class_1921}---Jeremiah 30:11, READ IT!

Daniel ends this part of his prayer with a reference to God delivering Israel from Egypt at the Red Sea. The reason he does that is because that is what Moses did whenever the Lord was ready to wipe out those Jews in the wilderness. God would get mad at them for some sin they committed and say to Moses, "Stand back! I'm going to get rid of every one of them and start over with you!" And Moses would say, "Lord, you know if you do that, those Egyptians and Canaanites will say you may have been able to get your people through the Red Sea, but you couldn't get them into the Promised Land. Lord, if you do this thing, your name will be MUD among the heathen. You had better [repent,]{.class_1921} Lord" (read Exod. 32: 9--12; Num. 14:11--19). And God would back off and do something else.

That's what Daniel is doing here. He's saying, "Lord, we've sinned; we blew it. But you brought us out of Egypt to give us the Promised Land. Please forgive us and restore us so these heathen don't think they did all these awful things of their own accord." []{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1271.xhtml_page_211}Rabshakeh tried making that case for the King of Assyria---that the Lord wasn't able to stand against Sennacherib (see 2 Kings 18:33--35). The Angel of the Lord killed 185,000 Assyrians in one night for it (2 Kings 19:35).

If you are anti-Semitic, I am going to give you some sound advice that you can take or leave at your own peril. You had better keep your hands off that Jew. I know a lot of them are atheists, and most of them are Christ-rejectors, but you had better leave them alone. God may use a heathen nation to judge His people, but He hasn't forgotten the promise He made to Abraham, that got passed on to the twelve tribes (Gen. 12:3; Num. 24:9): God will still bless a nation that blesses that Jew, and He will still [curse]{.class_1921} a nation or individual who curses that Jew. America has been living off the blessings of previous generations that blessed the Jewish people. But under Clinton's "legacy" and Bush's "roadmap to peace" and Obama's appeasing his Moslem buddies, this nation has entered God's [curse.]{.class_1921} God may have used Babylon to judge Jerusalem and Judah, but once He was done with it, He said, ["happy shall he be, that rewardeth thee as thou hast served us. Happy shall he be, that taketh and dasheth thy little ones against the stones"]{.class_1922} (Psa. 137:8--9). You want to turn over the land God gave those Jews to a bunch of Moslems? Then the Lord will turn over your nation to a bunch of Moslems. Count on it!

16 O Lord, according to all thy righteousness, I beseech thee, let thine anger and thy fury be turned away from thy city Jerusalem, thy holy mountain: because for our sins, and for the iniquities of our fathers, Jerusalem and thy people are become a reproach to all that are about us.

17 Now therefore, O our God, hear the prayer of thy servant, and his supplications, and cause thy face to shine upon thy sanctuary that is desolate, for the Lord's sake.

18 O my God, incline thine ear, and hear; open thine eyes, and behold our desolations, and the city which is called by thy name: for we do not present our supplications before thee for our righteousnesses, but for thy great mercies.

19 O Lord, hear; O Lord, forgive; O Lord, hearken and do; defer not, for thine own sake, O my God: for thy city and thy people are called by thy name.

For eleven verses, Daniel has been confessing sin; now, in the last four verses of the prayer, he is ready to ask for forgiveness. That's nearly three to one [negative.]{.class_1921} The New Testament Gospel is ["that Christ died]{.class_1922} \[negative\][ for our sins ]{.class_1922}\[negative\][ . . . And that he was buried ]{.class_1922}\[negative\][, and that he rose again the third day ]{.class_1922}\[positive\]["]{.class_1922} (1 Cor. 15:3--4). Any preacher that isn't at least three-quarters [negative]{.class_1921} in his preaching isn't a Bible preacher. He may be some Pollyanna, motivational, feel-good speaker; but a Bible preacher he is not.

Notice that Daniel bases his appeal for forgiveness on God's righteousness (vs. 16), not his own or the nation's (vs. 18). Of course, this is not quite like the imputed righteousness of the New Testament. In the New Testament, God, in His mercy, saves you (Tit. 3:5) by offering you His righteousness as a free gift through His Son (Rom. 5:18; 2 Cor. 5:21), which you receive by faith (Eph. 2:8--9). The righteousness of God referred to here in Daniel 9:16 is God doing right based on what He said in His word. Daniel is asking God to forgive and show mercy in order to keep His word as revealed to Jeremiah.

Daniel asks God to turn His wrath away from Jerusalem because the city and the Jews are a [disgrace]{.class_1921} (["a reproach"]{.class_1922}) to all the heathen nations about them. Those lost Gentiles are passing by that city left in ashes and rubble, with a few poor people left in it to survive off what the land brings forth on its own, and they are hissing at the place like you would a villain in the movies (1 Kings 9:8). They look at that mess, and someone says, "Isn't that mountain of ashes over there what's left of the Lord's Temple?" His buddy says, "Yep, that's it." "Well, why did God let it be burnt to the ground if He's so powerful and all?" asks the first fellow. And the second guy replies, "Don't you know? Those Jews started serving other gods, and that's how a jealous God repays a bunch of ingrates who forget how He delivered them out of Egypt." Go read Deuteronomy 29:25--28 and 1 Kings 9:7--9, and see if that's not the case.

Now, having gone through all that once, you would think those Jews would have enough sense not to go through it a second time. But you are about to read down in verse 26 about their Messiah coming and being killed, and the Temple and the city being destroyed [again.]{.class_1921} Why? Because they rejected their Messiah for [their own self-righteousness]{.class_1921} (read Matt. 23 and notice vss. 3--5 and vss. 37--39). Those who found mercy during Christ's ministry were the ones who admitted they were sinners and forsook their own self-righteousness (Luke 23:41, 18:1[0]{.class_1927}--14).

["Cause thy face to shine upon thy sanctuary that is desolate"---]{.class_1922}that places part of Daniel's prayer squarely in the Tribulation. The ["sanctuary"]{.class_1922} is made ["desolate"]{.class_1922} by the Antichrist (see our comments on 8:13). At the end of the Tribulation, a plague of darkness is poured out on the kingdom of the Antichrist (Rev. 16:10), and like the plague of darkness in Egypt (Exod. 10:21), the one in the Tribulation can ["be felt"]{.class_1922}---men gnaw ["their tongues for pain."]{.class_1922} This darkness can only be dispelled when ["the Sun of righteousness ]{.class_1922}\[shall\][ arise with healing in his wings"]{.class_1922} (Mal. 4:2). So the prayer of the Jews at that time will be for Jesus Christ to ["Arise, shine"]{.class_1922} (Isa. 60:1--2), because when He does, He will save them (Psa. 80:1, 3, 7, 19), both physically from the Antichrist's armies (Mal. 4:3) and spiritually as well (Rom. 11:25--27).

Take note of what Daniel calls Jerusalem in verse 18: ["the city which is called by THY NAME."]{.class_1922} That ["name"]{.class_1922} is NOT "Allah," which isn't a name at all. All the word [Allah]{.class_1921} means is "the God." [God]{.class_1921} is not a name any more than [human]{.class_1921} is for a man. A man has a name: Peter, Ralph, Joe, Frank, Tom, etc. He's not called "the man" or "the human." The God of the Bible has a [name.]{.class_1921} In the Old Testament, that name is [Jehovah]{.class_1921} (Exod. 6:3), translated quite often in your [King James]{.class_1921} Bible as ["LORD."]{.class_1922} So in the Old Testament, Jerusalem is called ["the city of the LORD . . . the city of OUR God"]{.class_1922} (Psa. 48:8). Whose ["God"]{.class_1922}? The god of Mohammed and the Moslems? Don't be stupid! He's the God of [Israel:]{.class_1921}[ "The city of the LORD, The Zion of the Holy One of ISRAEL"]{.class_1922} (Isa. 60:14).

The Mohammedan fares no better in the New Testament, for there, God's name is [Jesus Christ]{.class_1921} (1 John 5:20). Jesus Christ called Jerusalem ["the city of the great King"]{.class_1922} (Matt. 5:35). Who's ["the great King"]{.class_1922}? [He's]{.class_1921}[ "the great King"]{.class_1922}[]{#i4F9B8-8TQm_cNiaQPK_vw1271.xhtml_page_214} (1 Tim. 6:14--15; Rev. 17:14, 19:16, 20:4, 6).

So there is no "two-State solution" for Palestine or Jerusalem. God's plan for every Mohammedan from Egypt to Iraq, and from Turkey to Saudi Arabia (Gen. 15:18), is [utter destruction]{.class_1921} (Psa. 101:8). Jerusalem will be not only the capital of the nation of Israel, but the capital of the whole world, ruled over by a [Judean Jew]{.class_1921} (Zech. 14:3--4, 9, 16--21). In ["that day,"]{.class_1922} the city will literally be called by the name of the Lord, for it will be called ["Jehovah-shammah"]{.class_1921}---["The LORD is there"]{.class_1922} (Ezek. 48:35)---because Jehovah incarnate is on the throne. It will also be called ["Jehovah-tsidkenu"]{.class_1921}---["The LORD our righteousness"]{.class_1922} (Jer. 33:16)---because Jehovah incarnate was the One who saved them and gave them His righteousness (Rom. 11:26--27).

Verse 18: ["O my God"]{.class_1922}; notice it again in verse 19: ["O my God."]{.class_1922} That has probably become the most common form of taking the Lord's name in vain (see Exod. 20:7)---i.e., meaningless, without purpose---that you see nowadays. You will see it on kids' cartoon shows nowadays, and hear children as young as five years old saying it. It has been shortened to "OMG" on the "Internet."

But that is not something to be said lightly.
